END LDAP_UTIL;
/





create or replace PACKAGE BODY                      "LDAP_UTIL" AS

 --******************************************************************************
 --LDAP-Infos in Tabelle liefern
 --******************************************************************************

    function fLdapSearch(
        aSurname in varchar2,
        aGivenname in varchar2 default null,
        aSubdept in varchar2 default null,
        aMail in varchar2 default null,
        aGid in varchar2 default null
    ) return t_ldap_table as
    
        cLdapHost constant varchar2(250) := 'zebra.in.audi.vwg';
        cLdapPort constant number := 1636;
        cLdapBase constant varchar2(250) := 'DC=vwg,DC=com';
        cWallet constant varchar2(250) := 'file:/u00/app/oracle/admin/P181/wallet/VORSCHRIFTEN';
        cWalletPWD constant varchar2(250) := 'pw4+wallet+VORS+P';
        cLDAPBindUser constant varchar2(250) := 'cn=regulation_index,o=Adm,dc=Audi,dc=vwg,dc=com';
        cLDAPBindPass constant varchar2(250) := '02m5&trrpotvA2F9';
        lLdapFilter varchar2(250);
        lReturnValue number;
        lUserCount number;
        lLdapSession DBMS_LDAP.session;
        lLdapMessage DBMS_LDAP.message;
        lAttributeName varchar2(250);
        lLdapEntry DBMS_LDAP.message;
        lLdapElement DBMS_LDAP.ber_element;
        lAttributes DBMS_LDAP.string_collection;
        lValues DBMS_LDAP.STRING_COLLECTION;
        lLdapRow t_ldap_col;
        lLdapTable t_ldap_table := t_ldap_table();    
        
    begin

        lLdapFilter := '(&(sn=' || aSurname || '*)(givenname=' || aGivenname || '*)(subdepartment=' || aSubdept || '*)';
        if (aMail is not null) then
            lLdapFilter := lLdapFilter || '(mail=' || aMail || '*)';
        end if;
        lLdapFilter := lLdapFilter || '(gid=' || aGid || '*))';


        dbms_ldap.use_exception := true;
    
        lLdapSession := dbms_ldap.init(cLdapHost,cLdapPort);
    
        lReturnValue := DBMS_LDAP.open_ssl(
                ld              => lLdapSession,
                sslwrl          => cWallet,
                sslwalletpasswd => cWalletPWD,
                sslauth         => 2 );

        lReturnValue := dbms_ldap.simple_bind_s(lLdapSession, cLDAPBindUser, cLDAPBindPass); 

        lAttributes(1) := 'telephoneNumber';
        lAttributes(2) := 'subdepartment';
        lAttributes(3) := 'mail';
        lAttributes(4) := 'givenName';
        lAttributes(5) := 'sn';
        lAttributes(6) := 'employeeNumber';
        lAttributes(7) := 'costCenter';
        lAttributes(8) := 'ntPrimaryUserAccount';
        lAttributes(9) := 'l';
        lAttributes(10):= 'gid';

        lAttributes(11) := 'roomNumber';
        lAttributes(12) := 'subDepartmentLong';
        lAttributes(13) := 'cn';

        lReturnValue := DBMS_LDAP.search_s(lLdapSession, cLdapBase, DBMS_LDAP.SCOPE_SUBTREE, lLdapFilter, lAttributes, 0, lLdapMessage);
        lUserCount := DBMS_LDAP.count_entries(lLdapSession, lLdapMessage);

        lLdapEntry := DBMS_LDAP.first_entry(lLdapSession, lLdapMessage);

        while lLdapEntry IS NOT NULL
        loop

            lAttributeName := DBMS_LDAP.first_attribute(lLdapSession,lLdapEntry,lLdapElement);
            lLdapRow := t_ldap_col(null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null);

            WHILE lAttributeName IS NOT NULL
            LOOP

                lValues := DBMS_LDAP.get_values (lLdapSession, lLdapEntry, lAttributeName);

                IF (lValues.count > 0) THEN

                    case lAttributeName
                        when 'gid' then lLdapRow.GID:= lValues(0);
                        when 'sn' then lLdapRow.surname := lValues(0);
                        when 'givenName' then lLdapRow.givenName := lValues(0);
                        when 'subDepartment' then lLdapRow.SUBDEPARTMENT := lValues(0);
                        when 'mail' then lLdapRow.mail := lValues(0);
                        when 'telephoneNumber' then lLdapRow.phone := lValues(0);
                        else null;
                    end case;

                end if;

                lAttributeName := DBMS_LDAP.next_attribute(lLdapSession,lLdapEntry,lLdapElement);

            end loop;

            lLdapTable.extend();
            lLdapTable(lLdapTable.count) := lLdapRow;

            lLdapEntry := DBMS_LDAP.next_entry(lLdapSession, lLdapEntry);

        end loop;

        lReturnValue := DBMS_LDAP.unbind_s(lLdapSession);

        return lLdapTable;

    exception
        when others then
            lLdapRow := t_ldap_col(GID           => 'XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX',
                                   SURNAME       => 'ACL',
                                   GIVENNAME     => 'Freischaltung',
                                   SUBDEPARTMENT => 'Zebra',
                                   MAIL          => 'fehlt',
                                   PHONE         => '',
                                   COSTCENTER    => '',
                                   EN            => '');
            lLdapTable := t_ldap_table();
            lLdapTable.extend();
            lLdapTable(1) := lLdapRow;
            return lLdapTable;

    end fLdapSearch;        


    function fLdapSearchAlt(
        aSurname in varchar2,
        aGivenname in varchar2 default null,
        aSubdept in varchar2 default null,
        aMail in varchar2 default null,
        aGid in varchar2 default null
    ) return t_ldap_table as

        cLdapHost constant varchar2(250) := 'zebra.in.audi.vwg';
        cLdapPort constant number := 1389;
        cLdapBase constant varchar2(250) := 'DC=Audi,DC=vwg,DC=com';
        lLdapFilter varchar2(250);
        lReturnValue number;
        lUserCount number;
        lLdapSession DBMS_LDAP.session;
        lLdapMessage DBMS_LDAP.message;
        lAttributeName varchar2(250);
        lLdapEntry DBMS_LDAP.message;
        lLdapElement DBMS_LDAP.ber_element;
        lAttributes DBMS_LDAP.string_collection;
        lValues DBMS_LDAP.STRING_COLLECTION;
        lLdapRow t_ldap_col;
        lLdapTable t_ldap_table := t_ldap_table();

    begin

        lLdapFilter := '(&(sn=' || aSurname || '*)(givenname=' || aGivenname || '*)(subdepartment=' || aSubdept || '*)';
        if (aMail is not null) then
            lLdapFilter := lLdapFilter || '(mail=' || aMail || '*)';
        end if;
        lLdapFilter := lLdapFilter || '(gid=' || aGid || '*))';

        DBMS_LDAP.USE_EXCEPTION := TRUE;
        lLdapSession := DBMS_LDAP.init(cLdapHost,cLdapPort);
        lReturnValue := DBMS_LDAP.simple_bind_s(lLdapSession,null, null);

        lAttributes(1) := 'telephoneNumber';
        lAttributes(2) := 'subdepartment';
        lAttributes(3) := 'mail';
        lAttributes(4) := 'givenName';
        lAttributes(5) := 'sn';
        lAttributes(6) := 'employeeNumber';
        lAttributes(7) := 'costCenter';
        lAttributes(8) := 'ntPrimaryUserAccount';
        lAttributes(9) := 'l';
        lAttributes(10):= 'gid';

        lAttributes(11) := 'roomNumber';
        lAttributes(12) := 'subDepartmentLong';
        lAttributes(13) := 'cn';

        lReturnValue := DBMS_LDAP.search_s(lLdapSession, cLdapBase, DBMS_LDAP.SCOPE_SUBTREE, lLdapFilter, lAttributes, 0, lLdapMessage);
        lUserCount := DBMS_LDAP.count_entries(lLdapSession, lLdapMessage);

        lLdapEntry := DBMS_LDAP.first_entry(lLdapSession, lLdapMessage);

        while lLdapEntry IS NOT NULL
        loop

            lAttributeName := DBMS_LDAP.first_attribute(lLdapSession,lLdapEntry,lLdapElement);
            lLdapRow := t_ldap_col(null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null);

            WHILE lAttributeName IS NOT NULL
            LOOP

                lValues := DBMS_LDAP.get_values (lLdapSession, lLdapEntry, lAttributeName);

                IF (lValues.count > 0) THEN

                    case lAttributeName
                        when 'gid' then lLdapRow.GID:= lValues(0);
                        when 'sn' then lLdapRow.surname := lValues(0);
                        when 'givenName' then lLdapRow.givenName := lValues(0);
                        when 'subDepartment' then lLdapRow.SUBDEPARTMENT := lValues(0);
                        when 'mail' then lLdapRow.mail := lValues(0);
                        when 'telephoneNumber' then lLdapRow.phone := lValues(0);
                        else null;
                    end case;

                end if;

                lAttributeName := DBMS_LDAP.next_attribute(lLdapSession,lLdapEntry,lLdapElement);

            end loop;

            lLdapTable.extend();
            lLdapTable(lLdapTable.count) := lLdapRow;

            lLdapEntry := DBMS_LDAP.next_entry(lLdapSession, lLdapEntry);

        end loop;

        lReturnValue := DBMS_LDAP.unbind_s(lLdapSession);

        return lLdapTable;

    exception
        when others then
            lLdapRow := t_ldap_col(GID           => 'XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX',
                                   SURNAME       => 'ACL',
                                   GIVENNAME     => 'Freischaltung',
                                   SUBDEPARTMENT => 'Zebra',
                                   MAIL          => 'fehlt',
                                   PHONE         => '',
                                   COSTCENTER    => '',
                                   EN            => '');
            lLdapTable := t_ldap_table();
            lLdapTable.extend();
            lLdapTable(1) := lLdapRow;
            return lLdapTable;

    end fLdapSearchAlt;
   procedure syncronizeUserDatawithLDAP is

  snachname T_Benutzer.nachname%type;
  svorname T_Benutzer.vorname%type;
  sabteilung T_Benutzer.abteilung%type;
  semail T_Benutzer.email%type;
  sphone T_Benutzer.telefon%type;
  icounter number :=0;
 BEGIN
  FOR cu IN (select gid, letzte_aenderung_datum from T_Benutzer where gid is not null and gid != '5' and status = 10 for update) Loop
    if (cu.gid is null) then 
       continue;
    end if;
    begin
      select surname, givenname, subdepartment, mail, phone 
      into snachname, svorname, sabteilung, semail, sphone
      from Table(ldap_util.fLdapSearch( aSurname => null, aGid => cu.gid));

      EXCEPTION
       WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
       --dbms_output.put_line('no data found for ' || cu.gid ||  ', changed ' || to_char(cu.letzte_aenderung_datum, 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi:ss'));
        continue;
    end;

    UPDATE T_Benutzer SET --nachname = snachname, vorname = svorname,  
    abteilung = sabteilung /*,
         email = semail, telefon = sphone  */
    WHERE gid = cu.gid 
      AND ( /*nvl(nachname,'#') != nvl(snachname,'#') OR nvl(vorname,'#') != nvl(svorname,'#') OR */
      nvl(abteilung,'#') != nvl(sabteilung,'#') /*OR
         nvl(email,'#') != nvl(semail,'#') OR nvl(telefon,'#') != nvl(sphone,'#')*/
         );
    --dbms_output.put_line(' found ' || snachname || ', ' || svorname || ' for ' || cu.gid ||  ', changed ' || to_char(cu.letzte_aenderung_datum, 'dd.mm.yyyy hh24:mi:ss'));
   icounter := icounter+1;
  END LOOP;
  commit;
  dbms_output.put_line(' syncronized: ' || to_char(icounter) );
END syncronizeUserDatawithLDAP;

END LDAP_UTIL;
/

create or replace PACKAGE "PCK_AK" AS 

    function fValidateDeleteVKO(aETB_AK_REF_BENUTZERID in number) return varchar2;


END PCK_AK;
/


create or replace PACKAGE BODY "PCK_AK" AS

    function fValidateDeleteVKO(aETB_AK_REF_BENUTZERID in number) return varchar2 AS
        lAKID number;
        lBenutzerid number;
        lAnzahl number;
        lArbeitskreise varchar2(250);
    BEGIN
        select et_b_akid, benutzerid into lAKID, lBenutzerid
        from t_et_b_ak_ref_benutzer
        where et_b_ak_ref_benutzerid = aETB_AK_REF_BENUTZERID;

        -- Je Vorschrift, in denen der VKO Lead ist:
        for v in (select vorschriftid, vorschrift_nummer from t_vorschrift where lead_vko_benutzerid = lBenutzerid) loop

            with cte1 as (
                -- Arbeitskreise der Vorschrift
                select et_b_akid
                from t_vorschrift_ref_et_b_ak r
                where r.vorschriftid = v.vorschriftid and geloescht = 0

                intersect

                -- Arbeitskreise die beim Benutzer nach dem Löschvorgang übrig sind
                select et_b_akid
                from t_et_b_ak_ref_benutzer
                where benutzerid = lBenutzerid and et_b_akid != lAKID
            )
            select count(*) into lAnzahl
            from cte1;

            if (lAnzahl = 0) then
                -- Es bleibt nach dem Löschvorgang keine Schnittmenge übrig, Löschvorgang ist daher nicht erlaubt
                select listagg(ak.kurz, ', ') within group (order by ak.kurz) into lArbeitskreise
                from t_et_b_ak_ref_benutzer r
                join t_et_b_ak ak on (r.et_b_akid = ak.et_b_akid)
                where r.benutzerid = lBenutzerid;
                return 'Der Anwender ist den Arbeitskreisen ' || lArbeitskreise || ' als VKO zugeordnet. Der Löschvorgang ist daher wegen der Vorschrift ' || v.vorschrift_nummer || ' nicht erlaubt!';
            end if;

        end loop;

        RETURN null;
    END fValidateDeleteVKO;

END PCK_AK;
/

    -- Auto-update open tickets - Start

    PROCEDURE pUpdateOpenTickets(
        p_vorschriftid NUMBER
    );

    -- Update individual MfV ticket
    PROCEDURE pUpdateMfVTicket(
        p_mfvid NUMBER
    );

    -- Auto-update open tickets - end















  
END PCK_CIP_JIRA;
/

 from dual;

  procedure ploadCIPJira AS
  BEGIN
  debug('MFV-Beladung','Start MFV-Beladung');
  
for c in (Select mfv_cip_tmpid from t_x_mfv_cip_tmp)
loop  
MERGE INTO t_x_mfv_cip tm
USING (
 
              SELECT
                  x.*,t.*
 
 
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip_tmp t, 
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$.issues[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
                              restjson CLOB FORMAT JSON PATH '$',
                               jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key',
                              jiraid VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.id',
                             lastupdate date path '$.fields.updated'
                          )
                      )
                  x
 
 
                  where t.mfv_cip_tmpid = c.mfv_cip_tmpid
                  ) u
 on (tm.jira_key =u.jirakey)   
 when matched then update set tm.LAST_CHECKED =u.LAST_CHECKED, mfv_data_clob =u.restjson, tm.LAST_UPDATE = u.lastupdate
when not matched then insert (mfv_data_clob,ZEITPUNKT,JIRA_KEY,LAST_CHECKED,LAST_UPDATE)
values(u.restjson,sysdate,u.jirakey,sysdate,sysdate); 
commit;
 
 
delete from t_x_mfv_cip_tmp t where t.mfv_cip_tmpid = c.mfv_cip_tmpid ;
end loop;
 
 
 
-- Einfügen neuer MFVs
MERGE INTO t_mfv tm
USING (
          WITH cte1 AS (
              SELECT /*+ MATERIALIZE */
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
 
 
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
                              json VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$',
                              jiraid VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.id', issuetypeid number path '$.fields.issuetype.id',
                              mfv_name VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_11635',
                       --cf19470 varchar2(250) path '$.fields.customfield_19470',
                       --cf10288 varchar2(250) path '$.fields.customfield_10288',
                              NESTED PATH '$.fields.customfield_16813[*]'
                                  COLUMNS (
                                      mfv_teil VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.value'
                                  ),--  Teil
                     /*  nested path '$.fields.customfield_18109[*]'  columns(
                       AKTIVITAET varchar2(250) path '$.value' ),*/
                              thema VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.summary'            -- Thema der MfV
                              ,
                              beteiligte_oes VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_17002'   -- abteilung OE
                              ,
                              status_umgebung VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.environment'        -- Umgebung-status
                              ,
                              linksammelordner VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_17321'
                      /* ,  nested path '$.fields.components[*]' columns(
                       AK_kurz   varchar2(250) path '$.name')*/,
                              vorschriftnummer_klar VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_18301',
                              vorschriftid VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_18411',
                              erstelldatum_jira VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.created',
                              jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key',
                              status VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.status.name',
                              environment VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.environment'
                          )
                      )
                  x
              WHERE
                  substr(jirakey, 0, 4) = gENVIRONMENT and issuetypeid in (3,13733,14201) and mfv_teil not in ('Konzernweite Abstimmung')
          )
          SELECT DISTINCT
              t1.beteiligte_oes,
              t1.jirakey,
              t1.thema mfv_thema,
              t1.mfv_name,
              t1.environment,
       --       aktivitaet,
         /*     CASE
                  WHEN aktivitaet = 'Ohne MfV beendet' THEN
                      20
                  WHEN t1.status IN (
                      'Geschlossen',
                      'Geprüft',
                      'Freigabe'
                  ) THEN
                      10
                  ELSE
                      0
              END AS status_closed,*/
              tm.mfvid,
             trim( linksammelordner) linksammelordner
          FROM
              cte1    t1
              LEFT OUTER JOIN t_mfv   tm ON ( ( t1.jirakey = tm.jira_ticket ) )
        /*  WHERE 
          NOT EXISTS (
                  SELECT
                      1
                  FROM
                      cte1 t
                  WHERE
                      t1.jirakey = t.jirakey
                      AND t.mfv_teil IN (
                         'Konzernweite Abstimmung'
                      )
             )
*/
            /*  AND NOT EXISTS (
                  SELECT
                      1
                  FROM
                      cte1 t
                  WHERE
                      t1.jirakey = t.jirakey
                      AND t.ak_kurz IN (
                          'Testticket'
                      )
              )*/
-- and not exists (Select 1 from cte1 ta where t1.jiraid = ta.jiraid and ta.aktivitaet ='Ohne MfV beendet')
      )
u ON ( tm.mfvid = u.mfvid )
/*when matched then update set
 mf.mfv_teilid = u.mfv_teilid,
 mf.mfv_thema = u.mfv_thema,
mf.beteiligte_oes =u.beteiligte_oes,
mf.jira_ticket =u.jira_key,
mf.mfv_name = u.mfv_name, 
    mf.link_mfv_dms = u.linksammelordner,
  dms_dokumentenstatus =20  */
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
INSERT (
    beteiligte_oes,
    jira_ticket,
    mfv_thema,
    mfv_name,
    ksuid,
    dms_dokumentenstatus,
   -- jira_status,
    umgebungsstatus,
    link_mfv_dms)
VALUES
    ( u.beteiligte_oes,
      u.jirakey,
      u.mfv_thema,
      u.mfv_name,
    1020,
    20,
 --     u.status_closed,
      u.environment,
    TRIM(u.linksammelordner)
     );
 
--update alter MFVs
 
MERGE INTO t_mfv tm
USING ( with cte1 as (
         SELECT /*+ MATERIALIZE */
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
 
                    --case when status in ('Geschlossen','Geprüft','Freigabe')then 10 else 0 end as status_closed
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
                              json VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$',
                              jiraid VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.id', issuetypeid number path '$.fields.issuetype.id',
                              mfv_name VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_11635',
                       --cf19470 varchar2(250) path '$.fields.customfield_19470',
                       --cf10288 varchar2(250) path '$.fields.customfield_10288',
                              NESTED PATH '$.fields.customfield_16813[*]'
                                  COLUMNS (
                                      mfv_teil VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.value'
                                  ),--  Teil
                     /*  nested path '$.fields.customfield_18109[*]'  columns(
                       AKTIVITAET varchar2(250) path '$.value' ),*/
                              thema VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.summary'            -- Thema der MfV
                              ,
                              beteiligte_oes VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_17002'   -- abteilung OE
                              ,
                              status_umgebung VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.environment'        -- Umgebung-status
                              ,
                              linksammelordner VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_17321'
                      /* ,  nested path '$.fields.components[*]' columns(
                       AK_kurz   varchar2(250) path '$.name')*/,
                              vorschriftnummer_klar VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_18301',
                              vorschriftid VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_18411',
                              erstelldatum_jira VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.created',
                              jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key',
                              status VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.status.name',
                              environment VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.environment'
                          )
                      )
                  x
              WHERE
                  substr(jirakey, 0, 4) = gENVIRONMENT and issuetypeid in (3,13733,14201) --and mfv_teil not in ('Konzernweite Abstimmung')
          ), cte_old AS (
              SELECT DISTINCT
                  t1.beteiligte_oes,
                  t1.jirakey,
                  t1.thema mfv_thema,
                  t1.mfv_name,
                  t1.environment,
                 /* CASE
                      WHEN aktivitaet = 'Ohne MfV beendet' THEN
                          20
                      WHEN t1.status IN (
                          'Geschlossen',
                          'Geprüft',
                          'Freigabe'
                      ) THEN
                          10
                      ELSE
                          0
                  END AS status_closed,*/
                  tm.mfvid,
                  linksammelordner
              FROM
                  cte1    t1
                  LEFT OUTER JOIN t_mfv   tm ON ( ( t1.jirakey = tm.jira_ticket ) )
 
 
          )
          SELECT DISTINCT
              t1.beteiligte_oes,
              t1.jirakey,
              t1.mfv_thema, --tm.mfv_thema thema_old,
              t1.mfv_name,-- tm.mfv_name name_old,
              t1.environment,-- tm.UMGEBUNGSSTATUS UMGEBUNGSSTATUS_old,
            --  t1.status_closed, --tm. jira_status  status_closed_old
              t1.mfvid,
              t1.linksammelordner --, LINK_MFV_DMS
          FROM
              cte_old   t1
              LEFT OUTER JOIN t_mfv     tm ON ( t1.mfvid = tm.mfvid )
          WHERE
              nvl(t1.mfv_thema, 'A') != nvl(tm.mfv_thema, 'A')
              OR nvl(t1.mfv_name, 'A') != nvl(tm.mfv_name, 'A')
              OR t1.environment != tm.umgebungsstatus
            --  OR t1.status_closed != tm.jira_status
              OR TRIM(t1.linksammelordner) != tm.link_mfv_dms
      )
u ON ( tm.mfvid = u.mfvid )
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE
SET tm.umgebungsstatus = u.environment,
    tm.mfv_thema = u.mfv_thema,
  --  tm.jira_status = u.status_closed,
    tm.link_mfv_dms = TRIM(u.linksammelordner),
    tm.mfv_name = u.mfv_name;
 
--Ermitteln des Dokumentenstatus
MERGE INTO t_mfv tm
USING (  with cte1 as (
         SELECT /*+ MATERIALIZE */
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
 
                    --case when status in ('Geschlossen','Geprüft','Freigabe')then 10 else 0 end as status_closed
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
                              json VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$',
 
                             nested path '$.fields.customfield_18109[*]'  columns(
                                 AKTIVITAET varchar2(250) path '$.value' ),
                              status_umgebung VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.environment'        -- Umgebung-status
                              ,
                              linksammelordner VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_17321',
                              jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key',
                              issuetypeid number path '$.fields.issuetype.id',
                              status VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.status.name'
                          )
                      )
                  x
              WHERE issuetypeid in (13733,14201)
 
 
 
), cte2 as (
Select jirakey, case when AKTIVITAET = 'Ohne MfV beendet' then 40 when linksammelordner is not null and substr(trim(linksammelordner),0,5) = 'https'  and status in ('Geschlossen','Geprüft','Freigabe') then 20 else 10 end as status,
row_number() over (partition by jirakey order by case when AKTIVITAET = 'Ohne MfV beendet' then 1 else 999 end asc) xrow 
from cte1)
Select t2.jirakey, t2.status, tm.mfvid
from cte2  t2
LEFT OUTER JOIN t_mfv    tm ON ( t2.jirakey = tm.jira_ticket   )
where xrow = 1 and NVL(tm.dms_dokumentenstatus,10) != nvl(t2.status,10)
)
u ON ( tm.mfvid = u.mfvid )
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET
tm.dms_dokumentenstatus = u.status;
 
-- Einfügen der Labels
MERGE INTO t_mfv tm
USING ( with cte1 as (
         SELECT /*+ MATERIALIZE */
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
 
                    --case when status in ('Geschlossen','Geprüft','Freigabe')then 10 else 0 end as status_closed
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
 
                       nested path '$.fields.labels[*]'  columns(
                       labels varchar2(250) path '$'  ),
 
 
                              jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key'
 
                          )
                      )
                  x
 
          ), cte2 as (
          Select jirakey, listagg(labels,', ') within group (order by labels) schlagworte
          from cte1 t1
          group by jirakey
          )
          Select t2.jirakey, t2.schlagworte , tm.mfvid
          from cte2 t2
          LEFT OUTER JOIN t_mfv    tm ON ( t2.jirakey = tm.jira_ticket  )
          where nvl(t2.schlagworte,'1') != nvl(tm.schlagworte,'1')
          )
u ON ( tm.mfvid = u.mfvid )
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE
SET  tm.schlagworte = u.schlagworte;
-- Einfügen des Jira Status
  debug('MFV-Beladung','Jira-Status');
MERGE INTO t_mfv tm
USING ( with cte1 as (
         SELECT /*+ MATERIALIZE */
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
 
                    --case when status in ('Geschlossen','Geprüft','Freigabe')then 10 else 0 end as status_closed
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
  mfv_name VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_11635',
                       nested path '$.fields.customfield_18109[*]'  columns(
                       AKTIVITAET varchar2(250) path '$.value' ),
 
 
                              jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key',
                              status VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.status.name'
                          )
                      )
                  x
                  --where jirakey = 'TVRB-25767'
               --and mfv_teil not in ('Konzernweite Abstimmung')
          ), cte_res as (
              SELECT DISTINCT
            CASE 
                        WHEN aktivitaet = 'Ohne MfV beendet' and t1.mfv_name = 'ohne MfV' THEN
                          20
                      WHEN t1.status IN (
                          'Geschlossen',
                          'Geprüft',
                          'Freigabe'
                      ) THEN
                          10
                      ELSE
                          0
                  END AS status_closed,
                  tm.mfvid
              FROM
                  cte1    t1
                  LEFT OUTER JOIN t_mfv   tm ON ( ( t1.jirakey = tm.jira_ticket ) )
            where nvl(tm.jira_status,-1) != case WHEN aktivitaet = 'Ohne MfV beendet' THEN
                          20
                      WHEN t1.status IN (
                          'Geschlossen',
                          'Geprüft',
                          'Freigabe'
                      ) THEN
                          10
                      ELSE
                          0 end
)
Select mfvid, max(status_closed) status_closed
from cte_res
group by mfvid
 
 
      )
u ON ( tm.mfvid = u.mfvid )
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE
SET 
  tm.jira_status = u.status_closed
    ;
 
--Einfügen der Teile
 
MERGE INTO t_mfv_ref_mfv_teil tr
USING (
          WITH cte1 AS (
              SELECT /*+ MATERIALIZE */
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
 
                    --case when status in ('Geschlossen','Geprüft','Freigabe')then 10 else 0 end as status_closed
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
                              jiraid VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.id', issuetypeid number path '$.fields.issuetype.id',
                              mfv_name VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_11635',
                       --cf19470 varchar2(250) path '$.fields.customfield_19470',
                       --cf10288 varchar2(250) path '$.fields.customfield_10288',
                              NESTED PATH '$.fields.customfield_16813[*]'
                                  COLUMNS (
                                      mfv_teil VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.value',
                                      mf_teilid NUMBER PATH '$.id'
                                  ),--  Teil
 
                              jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key'
                          )
                      )
                  x
              WHERE
                  substr(jirakey, 0, 4) = gENVIRONMENT and issuetypeid in (3,13733,14201) and mfv_teil not in ('Konzernweite Abstimmung')
          )
          SELECT
              tm.mfvid,
              tmt.mfv_teilid,
              t1.mfv_teil
          FROM
              cte1         t1
              JOIN t_mfv        tm ON ( ( t1.jirakey = tm.jira_ticket ) )
              LEFT JOIN t_mfv_teil   tmt ON (( t1.mfv_teil = 'MfV Teil ' || tmt.teil and t1.issuetypeid = 3)or (tmt.teil = 1 and t1.issuetypeid = 13733) or (tmt.teil = 2 and t1.issuetypeid = 14201))
          WHERE
              t1.mfv_teil IS NOT NULL and tmt.mfv_teilid is not null
 
--and t1.mfv_name is not null --and t1.ak_kurz != 'Testticket' 
      )
u ON ( tr.mfvid = u.mfvid
       AND tr.mfv_teilid = u.mfv_teilid )
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
INSERT (
    mfvid,
    mfv_teilid )
VALUES
    ( u.mfvid,
      u.mfv_teilid );
-- löschen der nicht mehr vorhandenen Teile
 
delete from t_mfv_ref_mfv_teil tr
where mfv_ref_mfv_teilid in  (
          WITH cte1 AS (
              SELECT /*+ MATERIALIZE */
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
 
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
                              jiraid VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.id', issuetypeid number path '$.fields.issuetype.id',
                              mfv_name VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_11635',
 
                              NESTED PATH '$.fields.customfield_16813[*]'
                                  COLUMNS (
                                      mfv_teil VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.value',
                                      mf_teilid NUMBER PATH '$.id'
                                  ),--  Teil
 
                              jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key'
                          )
                      )
                  x
              WHERE
                  substr(jirakey, 0, 4) = gENVIRONMENT and issuetypeid in (3,13733,14201) and mfv_teil not in ('Konzernweite Abstimmung')
          ),cte_list as (
          SELECT
              tm.mfvid,
              tmt.mfv_teilid,
              t1.mfv_teil
          FROM
              cte1         t1
              JOIN t_mfv        tm ON ( ( t1.jirakey = tm.jira_ticket ) )
              LEFT JOIN t_mfv_teil   tmt ON (( t1.mfv_teil = 'MfV Teil ' || tmt.teil and t1.issuetypeid = 3)or (tmt.teil = 1 and t1.issuetypeid = 13733) or (tmt.teil = 2 and t1.issuetypeid = 14201))
          WHERE
              t1.mfv_teil IS NOT NULL and tmt.mfv_teilid is not null
            )
            Select trt.mfv_ref_mfv_teilid 
            from t_mfv_ref_mfv_teil trt
            where exists (Select 1 from cte_list ctl where trt.mfvid = ctl.mfvid ) and not exists (Select 1 from  cte_list ctl where trt.mfvid = ctl.mfvid and trt.mfv_teilid= ctl.mfv_teilid ) 
 
      );
---Einfügen der einzelnen Arbeitskreise
 
MERGE INTO t_mfv_ref_et_b_ak tm
USING (
          WITH cte1 AS (
              SELECT /*+ MATERIALIZE */
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
 
                    --case when status in ('Geschlossen','Geprüft','Freigabe')then 10 else 0 end as status_closed
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
                              jiraid VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.id', issuetypeid number path '$.fields.issuetype.id',
                              mfv_name VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_11635',
                              NESTED PATH '$.fields.components[*]'
                                  COLUMNS (
                                      ak_kurz VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.name'
                                  ),
                              jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key'
                          )
                      )
                  x
              WHERE
                  substr(jirakey, 0, 4) = gENVIRONMENT and issuetypeid in (3,13733,14201)
          )
          SELECT
              teak.et_b_akid,
              tm.mfvid,
              mfv_ref_et_b_akid
          FROM
              cte1                t1
              JOIN t_mfv               tm ON ( ( t1.jirakey = tm.jira_ticket ) )
              JOIN t_et_b_ak           teak ON ( t1.ak_kurz = teak.kurz )
              LEFT OUTER JOIN t_mfv_ref_et_b_ak   tmr ON ( tm.mfvid = tmr.mfvid
                                                         AND teak.et_b_akid = tmr.et_b_akid )
      )
u ON ( tm.mfv_ref_et_b_akid = u.mfv_ref_et_b_akid )
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
INSERT (
    mfvid,
    et_b_akid )
VALUES
    ( u.mfvid,
      u.et_b_akid );
--Löschen der überzähligen AK auf test ausdokumentiert Aufgrund der falschen Nummern aus TVET

                    --case when status in ('Geschlossen','Geprüft','Freigabe')then 10 else 0 end as status_closed

-- nach nummer
 
MERGE INTO t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmr
USING (
          WITH cte1 AS (
              SELECT /*+ MATERIALIZE */
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
                              mfv_name VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_11635',
                              jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key',
                              ak_kurz VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.components.name',
                              vorschriftid VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_18411',
                              vorschriftnummer_klar VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_18301'
                          )
                      )
                  x
                    --where jirakey = 'TVRB-25171'
                        --,'TVRB-21716' and mfv_teil not in ('Konzernweite Abstimmung')
          ), cte2_lb AS (
              SELECT
                  mfv_name,
                  jirakey,
                  ak_kurz,
                  TRIM(regexp_substr(t.vorschriftid, '[^('
                                                     || CHR(13)
                                                     || CHR(10)
                                                     || ')]+', 1, levels.column_value)) AS vorschriftlink_einzeln,
                  levels.column_value
              FROM
                  cte1 t,
                  TABLE ( CAST(MULTISET(
                      SELECT
                          level
                      FROM
                          dual
                      CONNECT BY
                          level <= regexp_count(t.vorschriftid, '[^('
                                                                || CHR(13)
                                                                || CHR(10)
                                                                || ')]') + 1
                  ) AS sys.odcinumberlist) ) levels
              WHERE
                  instr(t.vorschriftid, ',') = 0
          ), cte2_comma AS (
              SELECT
                  mfv_name,
                  jirakey,
                  ak_kurz,
                  TRIM(regexp_substr(t.vorschriftid, '[^,]+', 1, levels.column_value)) AS vorschriftlink_einzeln
              FROM
                  cte1 t,
                  TABLE ( CAST(MULTISET(
                      SELECT
                          level
                      FROM
                          dual
                      CONNECT BY
                          level <= regexp_count(t.vorschriftid, ',') + 1
                  ) AS sys.odcinumberlist) ) levels
              WHERE
                  instr(t.vorschriftid, ',') > 0
          ), cte2 AS (
              SELECT
                  mfv_name,
                  jirakey,
                  ak_kurz,
                  vorschriftlink_einzeln
              FROM
                  cte2_lb
                   where   vorschriftlink_einzeln is not null
              UNION
              SELECT
                  mfv_name,
                  jirakey,
                  ak_kurz,
                  vorschriftlink_einzeln
              FROM
                  cte2_comma
                  where   vorschriftlink_einzeln is not null
          ), cte3 AS (
              SELECT
                  tm.mfvid,
                 /* TRIM(regexp_replace(replace(vorschriftlink_einzeln, 'https://apps1.web.audi.vwg/apexaudi-sp/apex-sp/f?p=REGINDEX:VORSCHRIFT::::25:P25_VORSCHRIFTID:'
                  , ''), '[[:space:]]', '')) */
                   TRIM(regexp_replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(vorschriftlink_einzeln, 'https://apps1.web.audi.vwg/apexaudi-sp/apex-sp/f?p=REGINDEX:VORSCHRIFT::::25:P25_VORSCHRIFTID:',''),
                  'https://pre-apps1.web.audi.vwg/apexaudi-vt/apex-carmahvt/f?p=REGINDEX:VORSCHRIFT::::25:P25_VORSCHRIFTID:'
                  , ''),'https://pre-apps1.web.audi.vwg/apexaudi-tv/apex-carmahvt/f?p=REGINDEX:VORSCHRIFT::::25:P25_VORSCHRIFTID:',''),'https://apps1.web.audi.vwg/apexaudi-vp/apex-carmahvp/f?p=REGINDEX:VORSCHRIFT::::25:P25_VORSCHRIFTID:',''), '[[:space:]]', '')) AS vorschriftid,
                  t1.jirakey
              FROM
                  cte2    t1
                  JOIN t_mfv   tm ON ( ( t1.jirakey = tm.jira_ticket ) )
 
                                    --where t1.mfv_name is not null  
              WHERE
                  t1.jirakey != 'TVRB-19195'
          )
          SELECT
              t1.*,
              mfv_ref_vorschriftid
          FROM
              cte3                   t1
              LEFT OUTER JOIN t_mfv_ref_vorschrift   tm ON ( regexp_replace(TRIM(t1.vorschriftid),'\(.*\)' ) = tm.vorschriftid
                                                           AND t1.mfvid = tm.mfvid )
          WHERE
              t1.vorschriftid IS NOT NULL and   validate_conversion(t1.vorschriftid as NUMBER)=1
      )
u ON ( tmr.mfv_ref_vorschriftid = u.mfv_ref_vorschriftid )
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
INSERT (
    tmr.mfvid,
    tmr.vorschriftid )
VALUES
    ( u.mfvid,
      u.vorschriftid );
 --löschen alter nummern
 
delete from  t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmr
where mfv_ref_vorschriftid in(
          WITH cte1 AS (
              SELECT /*+ MATERIALIZE */
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
                              mfv_name VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_11635',
                              jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key',
                              ak_kurz VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.components.name',
                              vorschriftid VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_18411',
                              vorschriftnummer_klar VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_18301'
                          )
                      )
                  x
                    --where jirakey = 'TVRB-25171'
                        --,'TVRB-21716' and mfv_teil not in ('Konzernweite Abstimmung')
          ), cte2_lb AS (
              SELECT
                  mfv_name,
                  jirakey,
                  ak_kurz,
                  TRIM(regexp_substr(t.vorschriftid, '[^('
                                                     || CHR(13)
                                                     || CHR(10)
                                                     || ')]+', 1, levels.column_value)) AS vorschriftlink_einzeln,
                  levels.column_value
              FROM
                  cte1 t,
                  TABLE ( CAST(MULTISET(
                      SELECT
                          level
                      FROM
                          dual
                      CONNECT BY
                          level <= regexp_count(t.vorschriftid, '[^('
                                                                || CHR(13)
                                                                || CHR(10)
                                                                || ')]') + 1
                  ) AS sys.odcinumberlist) ) levels
              WHERE
                  instr(t.vorschriftid, ',') = 0
          ), cte2_comma AS (
              SELECT
                  mfv_name,
                  jirakey,
                  ak_kurz,
                  TRIM(regexp_substr(t.vorschriftid, '[^,]+', 1, levels.column_value)) AS vorschriftlink_einzeln
              FROM
                  cte1 t,
                  TABLE ( CAST(MULTISET(
                      SELECT
                          level
                      FROM
                          dual
                      CONNECT BY
                          level <= regexp_count(t.vorschriftid, ',') + 1
                  ) AS sys.odcinumberlist) ) levels
              WHERE
                  instr(t.vorschriftid, ',') > 0
          ), cte2 AS (
              SELECT
                  mfv_name,
                  jirakey,
                  ak_kurz,
                  vorschriftlink_einzeln
              FROM
                  cte2_lb
                   where   vorschriftlink_einzeln is not null
              UNION
              SELECT
                  mfv_name,
                  jirakey,
                  ak_kurz,
                  vorschriftlink_einzeln
              FROM
                  cte2_comma
                  where   vorschriftlink_einzeln is not null
          ), cte3 AS (
              SELECT
                  tm.mfvid,
                 /* TRIM(regexp_replace(replace(vorschriftlink_einzeln, 'https://apps1.web.audi.vwg/apexaudi-sp/apex-sp/f?p=REGINDEX:VORSCHRIFT::::25:P25_VORSCHRIFTID:'
                  , ''), '[[:space:]]', '')) */
                   TRIM(regexp_replace(replace(replace(replace(replace(vorschriftlink_einzeln, 'https://apps1.web.audi.vwg/apexaudi-sp/apex-sp/f?p=REGINDEX:VORSCHRIFT::::25:P25_VORSCHRIFTID:',''),
                  'https://pre-apps1.web.audi.vwg/apexaudi-vt/apex-carmahvt/f?p=REGINDEX:VORSCHRIFT::::25:P25_VORSCHRIFTID:'
                  , ''),'https://pre-apps1.web.audi.vwg/apexaudi-tv/apex-carmahvt/f?p=REGINDEX:VORSCHRIFT::::25:P25_VORSCHRIFTID:',''),'https://apps1.web.audi.vwg/apexaudi-vp/apex-carmahvp/f?p=REGINDEX:VORSCHRIFT::::25:P25_VORSCHRIFTID:',''), '[[:space:]]', '')) AS vorschriftid,
                  t1.jirakey
              FROM
                  cte2    t1
                  JOIN t_mfv   tm ON ( ( t1.jirakey = tm.jira_ticket ) )
 
                                    --where t1.mfv_name is not null  
              WHERE
                  t1.jirakey != 'TVRB-19195'
          ), cte_list as (
          SELECT
              t1.*,
              mfv_ref_vorschriftid
          FROM
              cte3                   t1
              LEFT OUTER JOIN t_mfv_ref_vorschrift   tm ON ( regexp_replace(TRIM(t1.vorschriftid),'\(.*\)' ) = tm.vorschriftid
                                                           AND t1.mfvid = tm.mfvid )
          WHERE
              t1.vorschriftid IS NOT NULL and   validate_conversion(t1.vorschriftid as NUMBER)=1
 
              ) select tmrv.mfv_ref_vorschriftid
              from t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv
               where exists (Select 1 from  cte_list ctl where ctl.mfvid = tmrv.mfvid) 
              and not exists (Select 1 from  cte_list ctl where ctl.mfvid = tmrv.mfvid and ctl.vorschriftid = tmrv.vorschriftid)  
 
      );

 von Nicht geprüft auf:
 Vorschrift hat nur NEIN Länder => Ignorieren
 Vorschrift-Land nur Ja und nur Ticket JA => automatisch auf JA
 Vorschrift-Land nur Ja und Tickets Nein => nein
 
 Vorschrift-Land gemsicht und nur Tickets = Ja => Ja
 Vorschrift-Land gemsicht und nur Tickets = nein => nein
 
 Alle Ja => customfield_17002 "OE2 des REVs"
 WIedersprechende Tickets => eintrag T_MFV_sums
 */
 /* Deaktiviert auf T aufgrund der Testtickets
 merge into t_vorschrift tv
 using  (
 with cte1 as (             SELECT 
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
 
 
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]?(@.fields.issuetype.id ==13732)'
                          COLUMNS (
                              json VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$',
                              jiraid VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.id',
                              issuetypeid number path '$.fields.issuetype.id',
                              sums_relevant VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_19317.value',  
                              jira_key_parent VARCHAR2(250) path '$.fields.issuelinks[0].outwardIssue.key',
                              jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key',
                              last_updated date path '$.fields.updated',
                               status VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.status.name'
                          )
                      )
                  x
              WHERE
                  substr(jirakey, 0, 4) = gENVIRONMENT and issuetypeid not in (3,13733,14201) and status in  (
                      'Geschlossen',
                      'Geprüft',
                      'Freigabe','Abgeschlossen'
                  )
 
                  ),cte_vorschrift as (
                  
                  Select tv.vorschriftid, sums_relevant
                  from t_vorschrift tv
                  left outer join  t_vorschrift_ref_land tvrl on (tv.vorschriftid = tvrl.vorschriftid and tvrl.geloescht = 0)
                  left outer join t_land tl on (tvrl.landid = tl.landid )
                  
                  ),cte_mfv_sums as (
                  Select case  t1.Sums_relevant when 'Not rated' then 20 when 'Yes' then 10 when 'No' then 0 else null end as mfv_RXSWIN,tmrv.vorschriftid
                  
                  from cte1 t1
                  join t_mfv tm on ( t1.jira_key_parent = tm.jira_ticket and tm.jira_status in ( 10,40) --and LETZTE_AENDERUNG_DATUM >= sysdate-50
                  )
                  join t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv on (tm.mfvid = tmrv.mfvid)
                  
                  
                  ),cte_mfv_sums_eindeutig as (
                  Select distinct vorschriftid, mfv_RXSWIN
                  from cte_mfv_sums t1
                  where not exists (Select 1 from cte_mfv_sums t2 where t1.vorschriftid = t2.vorschriftid and t1.mfv_RXSWIN != t2.mfv_RXSWIN)
                  
                  
                  
                  
                  ), cte2 as (
 
                  Select Sums_relevant,jira_key_parent, jirakey,tv.vorschriftid, tv.vorschrift_nummer, 
                  case tv.RXSWIN when 10 then 'ja' when 20 then 'Nicht geprüft' when 0 then 'nein' else 'n.n' end as Vorschriftsums
                  from cte1 t1
                  join t_mfv tm on ( t1.jira_key_parent = tm.jira_ticket and tm.jira_status in ( 10,40) --and LETZTE_AENDERUNG_DATUM >= sysdate-50
                  )
                  join t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv on (tm.mfvid = tmrv.mfvid)
                  join t_vorschrift tv on (tmrv.vorschriftid = tv.vorschriftid )
                  where not ('Not rated' =Sums_relevant and tv.RXSWIN = 20) and 
                  not ('Yes' =Sums_relevant and tv.RXSWIN = 10) and 
                  not ('No' =Sums_relevant and tv.RXSWIN = 0)
                  )
                  
                  Select vorschriftid, sums_relevant RXSWIN from cte_vorschrift
 
 ) u on (tv.vorschriftid = u.vorschriftid)
 when matched then update set
 tv.RXSWIN  = u.RXSWIN ;
 */
 -- Berechnung der Arbeitaufgaben

function fCreateJiraUrlAssistent(aVorschriftId NUMBER, aMFV_TEILID NUMBER,aAKIDS VARCHAR2 default null,aSchlagwörter VARCHAR2 default null, aZusVorschriften  VARCHAR2 default null, aMFVID VARCHAR2 default null, aprevMFVid number default null, aCocoaTicket VARCHAR2 default null) return clob as
      l_vs_nummer varchar2(4096);
      l_vs_bezeichnung varchar2(4096);
      l_vs_status varchar2(4096);
      l_vs_typid number;
      l_progn_quali varchar2(4096);
      l_datum_in_kraft varchar2(4096);
      l_datum_neuer_typ varchar2(4096);
      l_datum_alle_typen varchar2(4096);
      l_laender_fields varchar2(4096);
      l_ak_fields varchar2(4096);
      l_mfv varchar(4096);
      l_template varchar2(4096);
      l_issue_type varchar2(4096);
      l_labels varchar2(4096);
      l_vorschrift_old varchar2(4096);
      l_vorschrift_new varchar2(4096);
      l_vorschrift_permalink varchar2(4096);
      l_link  varchar2(4096);
      l_summary varchar2(4096);
      l_date_list varchar2(4096);
      l_land_list varchar2(4096);
      l_prevMFV varchar2(4096);
      l_SUMIS varchar2(4096);
      l_GETEX varchar2(4096);
       l_GETEX_ZUS varchar2(4096);
      l_anzpreMFV  number;
    l_customfield_53161 CLOB;
    l_customfield_53162 CLOB;
    l_customfield_53163 CLOB;
    l_json_array JSON_ARRAY_T;
l_json_array_land JSON_ARRAY_T;
l_json_array_ak JSON_ARRAY_T;
l_json_object_aufgabentyp_ak JSON_ARRAY_T;
l_json_object JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_land JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_ak JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_getex  JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_fields JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_project JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_issuetype JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_sums1 JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_sums2 JSON_OBJECT_T;
 l_json_object_prevMFV JSON_OBJECT_T;
 l_json_object_aufgabentyp       JSON_OBJECT_T; 
l_json_object_permalink JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_Dates JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_STATUS JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_MFVID JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_object_GETEX_URL JSON_OBJECT_T;
l_json_return JSON_OBJECT_T;
 
      l_return clob;
    begin
    -- 1 = Information , 2 = Entcheidung
    select case when aMFV_TEILID = 1 then '&issuetype=13733&customfield_16813=41540' else '&issuetype=14201&customfield_16813=41541' end,case when aMFV_TEILID = 1 then '&issueTemplateId=2936' else '&issueTemplateId=2935' end
    into l_issue_type,l_template
    from dual;
--Vorschriftnummer
    select v.vorschrift_nummer, v.vorschrift_bezeichnung,
      s.status, v.VORSCHRIFT_TYPID
    into l_vs_nummer, l_vs_bezeichnung,
      l_vs_status, l_vs_typid
    from t_vorschrift v
    left outer join t_vorschrift_status s on s.VORSCHRIFT_STATUSID = v.VORSCHRIFT_STATUSID
    where v.vorschriftid = aVorschriftId;
-- Vorschriftennummern neu & Permalinks
    with cte1 as (
    select  'Main regulation number: \r\n '|| v.vorschrift_nummer vorschrift_nummer,1 as sortorder, pck_ri.fCreatePermalinkUrl(vorschriftid) vorschriftlink
    ,  l_vs_status as vs_status
    from t_vorschrift v
    where v.vorschriftid = aVorschriftId
 
 
    )
 
    Select listagg(vorschrift_nummer,', \r\n ')within group (order by Sortorder asc, vorschrift_nummer asc), 
    listagg( vorschriftlink,',')within group (order by Sortorder asc, vorschrift_nummer asc)
 
    into l_vorschrift_new, l_vorschrift_permalink
    from cte1;
 
    with cte1 as (
    select v.vorschrift_nummer,2 as sortorder, pck_ri.fCreatePermalinkUrl(vorschriftid) vorschriftlink, s.status
    from t_vorschrift v
    left outer join t_vorschrift_status s on s.VORSCHRIFT_STATUSID = v.VORSCHRIFT_STATUSID
    where v.vorschriftid  in  (
                    SELECT
                        column_value
                    FROM
                        TABLE ( apex_string.split_numbers(aZusVorschriften , ':') )
                        ) and vorschriftid != aVorschriftId
                        )
    , cte2 as (Select listagg(vorschrift_nummer,', \r\n ')within group (order by Sortorder asc, vorschrift_nummer asc) vorschriftnummer, 
    listagg( vorschriftlink,', ')within group (order by Sortorder asc, vorschrift_nummer asc) vorschriftlink    
     ,listagg (vorschrift_nummer||': '|| Status, ', \r\n ')within group (order by Sortorder asc, vorschrift_nummer asc)  status
    from cte1)
    Select   nvl2(vorschriftnummer,l_vorschrift_new||'\r\n \r\n Additional regulation number(s): \r\n '||vorschriftnummer,l_vorschrift_new), 
    l_vorschrift_permalink || nvl2(vorschriftlink,', ' || vorschriftlink,'')
    ,  nvl2(vorschriftnummer,'Status main regulation: \r\n ' || l_vs_status ||'\r\n \r\n Status additional regulation(s): \r\n'|| status,'Status main regulation: \r\n ' || l_vs_status )
    into l_vorschrift_new, l_vorschrift_permalink 
    ,l_vs_status 
    from cte2;
-- GETEX Link 
SELECT 'Main regulation: \r\n ' ||
   -- replace(
    url_getex_vorschrift
    --, '+', '%2B') 
    ||'\r\n' into l_GETEX
FROM
    t_vorschrift
WHERE
    vorschriftid = avorschriftid;
SELECT
' \r\n Additional Regulations: \r\n ' ||
 listagg( vorschrift_nummer  || ': '|| --replace(
 url_getex_vorschrift
 --, '+', '%2B')
 ,' \r\n ' ON OVERFLOW TRUNCATE)within group ( order by vorschrift_nummer asc) into l_GETEX_zus
 FROM
     t_vorschrift
 WHERE
     vorschriftid IN (
         SELECT
             column_value
         FROM
             TABLE ( apex_string.split_numbers(azusvorschriften, ':') )
     )
      AND vorschriftid != avorschriftid
;
-- Vorgänger Vorschrift Old
    with cte1 as (Select vorschrift_nummer
    from t_vorschrift_ref_vorschrift tvrv
    join t_vorschrift tv on (tvrv.VORGAENGER_VORSCHRIFTID = tv.vorschriftid)
    where  beziehung_art = 10 and nachfolger_vorschriftid =aVorschriftId
    )
    Select case when aMFV_TEILID = 2 then '' else listagg(vorschrift_nummer, ', ') end into l_vorschrift_old 
    from cte1;
-- Prognose Qualität
    select case when v.prognose_qualitaet = 10 then 'sicher'
      when v.prognose_qualitaet = 20 then 'abschätzbar'
      else null
     end into l_progn_quali
    from T_VORSCHRIFT v
    where v.vorschriftid = aVorschriftId;
-- Ausgwäjlte Stichwörter
   /* Select listagg('&labels=' || replace(replace(aSchlagwörter,' ','_'),':','&labels='),'') into l_labels
    from dual;
 */
 
 Select  listagg(distinct Bezeichnung,', ') into l_labels
 from t_vorschrift_ref_thema tvrt
 join t_thema tt on (tvrt.themaid = tt.themaid)
 where tvrt.geloescht =0 and (tvrt.vorschriftid =  aVorschriftId or tvrt.vorschriftid IN (
         SELECT
             column_value
         FROM
             TABLE ( apex_string.split_numbers(azusvorschriften, ':') )) );
--Datumsangaben   
    select to_char(einsatzdatum, 'DD/MON/YY') into l_datum_in_kraft
    from t_vorschrift_ref_einsatzdatum_typ vre
 
    where vre.vorschriftid = aVorschriftId
        and vre.einsatzdatum_typid = 1000
    union all select null from dual
    fetch first 1 rows only;
 
    select listagg(case 
        when vre.einsatzdatum_typid = 1020 then 'CKD ' 
        when vre.einsatzdatum_typid = 1022 then 'FBU ' 
        else null
        end
        || to_char(einsatzdatum, 'DD/MON/YY'), ' ') within group (order by vre.einsatzdatum_typid) into l_datum_neuer_typ
    from t_vorschrift_ref_einsatzdatum_typ vre
    inner join t_vorschrift vs on (vs.vorschriftid = vre.vorschriftid)
    inner join t_einsatzdatum_typ edt on (edt.einsatzdatum_modellid = vs.einsatzdatum_modellid and vre.einsatzdatum_typid = edt.einsatzdatum_typid)
    where vre.vorschriftid = aVorschriftId
        and vre.einsatzdatum_typid in (1010, 1020, 1022, 1030)
    group by vs.vorschriftid
    union all select null from dual
    fetch first 1 rows only;
 
    select listagg(case 
        when vre.einsatzdatum_typid = 1021 then 'CKD ' 
        when vre.einsatzdatum_typid = 1023 then 'FBU ' 
        else null
        end
        || to_char(einsatzdatum, 'DD/MON/YY'), ' ') within group (order by vre.einsatzdatum_typid) into l_datum_alle_typen
    from t_vorschrift_ref_einsatzdatum_typ vre
    inner join t_vorschrift vs on (vs.vorschriftid = vre.vorschriftid)
    inner join t_einsatzdatum_typ edt on (edt.einsatzdatum_modellid = vs.einsatzdatum_modellid and vre.einsatzdatum_typid = edt.einsatzdatum_typid)
    where vre.vorschriftid = aVorschriftId
        and vre.einsatzdatum_typid in (1011, 1021, 1023, 1031)
    group by vs.vorschriftid
    union all select null from dual
    fetch first 1 rows only;
 
-- Datumsangaben als Liste
 
  select 'Application timing main regulation: \r\n  '|| listagg(EINSATZDATUM_TYP ||': '||case when  vre.EINSATZDATUM_TYPID in (1030,1031) and modeljahr is not null  then 'Modelljahr '||to_char(modeljahr, 'YYYY') else  to_char(einsatzdatum, 'DD.MM.YYYY') end,',\r\n') within group ( order by sortorder)into l_date_list
    from t_vorschrift_ref_einsatzdatum_typ vre
        join t_einsatzdatum_typ ty on (vre.einsatzdatum_typid = ty.einsatzdatum_typid)
    where vre.vorschriftid = aVorschriftId and einsatzdatum is not null and vre.EINSATZDATUM_TYPID  not in (1031)and (FAHRZEUGKLASSEID is null or FAHRZEUGKLASSEID = 1024)
   ;
 
-- Datumsangaben Zusätzliche Vorschriften
 
   with cte1 as (
   Select  ' \r\n '||VORSCHRIFT_NUMMER ||': \r\n ' ||listagg( EINSATZDATUM_TYP ||': '||case when  vre.EINSATZDATUM_TYPID in (1030,1031) and modeljahr is not null  then 'Modelljahr '||to_char(modeljahr, 'YYYY') else  to_char(einsatzdatum, 'DD.MM.YYYY') end,',\r\n \r\n') within group ( order by sortorder) as datum_angaben
   from t_vorschrift_ref_einsatzdatum_typ vre
        join t_einsatzdatum_typ ty on (vre.einsatzdatum_typid = ty.einsatzdatum_typid)
       join t_vorschrift v on (vre.vorschriftid = v.vorschriftid)
 
   where vre.vorschriftid  in  (
                    SELECT
                        column_value
                    FROM
                        TABLE ( apex_string.split_numbers(aZusVorschriften , ':') )
                        ) and vre.vorschriftid != aVorschriftId and einsatzdatum is not null  and vre.EINSATZDATUM_TYPID  not in (1031)and (FAHRZEUGKLASSEID is null or FAHRZEUGKLASSEID = 1024)
     group by VORSCHRIFT_NUMMER
    ),cte2 as (
    Select listagg(datum_angaben, '\r\n') datum_angaben
    from cte1
    )
    Select case when   datum_angaben is not null then  l_date_list || '\r\n \r\n Application timing additional regulation(s): \r\n \r\n '|| datum_angaben else l_date_list end into l_date_list
    from cte2;
 
    --Vorgänger MFV
    select count(*) into l_anzpreMFV
     from t_mfv
    where mfvid = aprevMFVid;
    if l_anzpreMFV >0 then 
            select mfv_name into l_prevMFV
 
            from t_mfv
            where mfvid = aprevMFVid;
    else
         l_prevMFV :='';
 end if;
    --mfv
    with mapped_mfvs as (
        select m.mfv_name
        from t_mfv_ref_vorschrift mrv
        join t_mfv m on m.mfvid = mrv.mfvid
        where mrv.vorschriftid = aVorschriftId
     )
    select nvl2(listagg(mfv_name, '/'), listagg(mfv_name,  '/') || ' ', aMFVID||' ') into l_mfv
    from mapped_mfvs;
-- Länder
  l_json_array_land := JSON_ARRAY_T();
 
 for c in (
 with land_jira_codes as (
     select distinct land.jira_code2 as jira_code
     from T_VORSCHRIFT_REF_LAND vtl 
     left outer join t_land land on land.landid = vtl.landid
     where (vtl.vorschriftid = aVorschriftId or vtl.vorschriftid in  (
                    SELECT
                        column_value
                    FROM
                        TABLE ( apex_string.split_numbers(aZusVorschriften , ':') )
                        ) )
      and vtl.geloescht = 0
      and land.jira_code2 is not null
    ), cte1 as (
 
 
select  land_jira_codes.jira_code
    from land_jira_codes
 union all
 Select 42225 from dual where l_vs_nummer like 'UN-R%'  or l_vs_typid = 20 or l_vs_nummer like 'GTR%' 
 )
 
 
 Select to_char(jira_code) jira_code
    from cte1
    )
    loop
     l_json_object_land := JSON_OBJECT_T();
    l_json_object_land.put('id' , c.jira_code);
    l_json_array_land.append( l_json_object_land);
 
    end loop;
   l_json_array_ak := JSON_ARRAY_T();
 
 for c in (
    /*with ak_jira_codes as ( -- AK-Kurzebez. muessen noch in Jira-IDs umgewandelt werden
     select distinct ak.JIRAID
     from  t_et_B_ak ak 
     where et_b_akid in  (
                    SELECT
                        column_value
                    FROM
                        TABLE ( apex_string.split_numbers(aAKIDS, ':') )
                        )
 
 
    )
    select JIRAID
     into l_ak_fields
    from ak_jira_codes*/
   -- Für Testumgebung
   with ak_jira_codes as ( -- AK-Kurzebez. muessen noch in Jira-IDs umgewandelt werden
     select 47649 as JIRAID
     from dual
 
 
    )
    select  to_char(JIRAID) JIRAID
 
    from ak_jira_codes
 
    )
 
    loop
    l_json_object_ak := JSON_OBJECT_T();
     l_json_object_ak.put('id' , c.jiraid);
        l_json_array_ak.append(l_json_object_ak);
 
    end loop;
 
-- Übetragung Sumis Relevant bei Information
if aMFV_TEILID=1
then
 
with cte1 as (
Select distinct vorschriftid, 1 as sums_land from t_vorschrift_ref_land tvrl
join t_land tl on (tvrl.landid = tl.landid)
where sums_relevant = 10
)
Select  case when rxswin = 10 and tv.homologationsrelevant = 10 and (nvl(sums_land,0) = 1 or substr(vorschrift_nummer,0,4) ='UN-R')then '54882'  
when rxswin = 0  and tv.homologationsrelevant = 10  then '54881' 
when rxswin = 20 and tv.homologationsrelevant = 10 and (nvl(sums_land,0) = 1 or substr(vorschrift_nummer,0,4) ='UN-R') then '63464' else '54881'  end into l_SUMIS
from t_vorschrift tv
left join cte1 t1 on (tv.vorschriftid = t1.vorschriftid)
where tv.vorschriftid =aVorschriftId;
else  
 l_SUMIS := '-1';
end if;
 
 
 
 
--Summary Abschneiden
with cte1 as(
 Select l_land_list|| ' - '||
 l_vs_nummer  as summary_text
 from dual
 ) Select case when length(summary_text) >= 250 then substr(summary_text,1,245)||'...' else summary_text end into l_summary
 from cte1;
 --24805 für P
l_json_object := JSON_OBJECT_T();
l_json_object_fields := JSON_OBJECT_T();
l_json_object_issuetype := JSON_OBJECT_T();
l_json_object_project := JSON_OBJECT_T();
l_json_object_sums1 := JSON_OBJECT_T();
l_json_object_sums2 := JSON_OBJECT_T();
l_json_object_prevMFV := JSON_OBJECT_T();
l_json_object_aufgabentyp := JSON_OBJECT_T();
 l_json_object_aufgabentyp_ak := JSON_ARRAY_T();   
 
l_json_object_project.put('id' , gENVIRONMENT_KEY);
l_json_object_getex := JSON_OBJECT_T();
l_json_object.put('customfield_16524' , nvl(l_GETEX || l_getex_zus,''));
 
l_json_object_aufgabentyp.put('id' , case when aMFV_TEILID = 1 then '41540' else '41541' end);
l_json_object_aufgabentyp_ak.append(l_json_object_aufgabentyp);
 
l_json_object.put ('customfield_16813',l_json_object_aufgabentyp_ak); 
l_json_object_issuetype.put('id',case when aMFV_TEILID = 1 then '13733' else '14201' end);
l_json_object.put ('project',l_json_object_project);
l_json_object.put ('issuetype' ,l_json_object_issuetype); 
l_json_object.put ('summary' ,l_summary);
l_json_object.put ('customfield_11643' , case when length(l_vs_bezeichnung) >= 250 then substr(l_vs_bezeichnung,1,245)||'...'  else l_vs_bezeichnung  end);
l_json_object_sums1.put('id' ,nvl(l_SUMIS,'-1') );
l_json_object.put( 'customfield_19317' ,l_json_object_sums1);
l_json_object.put('customfield_20204',l_prevMFV);
l_json_object.put( 'customfield_18422', nvl(l_vorschrift_old,' '));
l_json_object.put( 'customfield_18301' , nvl(l_vorschrift_new,' '));
l_json_object.put( 'customfield_18411' , nvl(l_vorschrift_permalink,' '));
l_json_object.put('customfield_11635', nvl(aMFVID,' '));
l_json_object.put( 'customfield_19700' , nvl(l_vs_status,' '));
l_json_object.put('customfield_10302' ,nvl(l_date_list,' '));
/*
if (aCocoaTicket is not null) 
then
for c in (SELECT
                  x.*,t.*
 
 
              FROM
                  t_x_cocoa_import t, 
                  JSON_TABLE ( data_clob, '$.fields[*]'
                          COLUMNS (

 --l_json_object :=
 l_json_object.put('customfield_18402',l_json_array_land);
 -- l_json_object.put('templateId',case when aMFV_TEILID = 1 then '2936' else '2935'end);
 l_json_object.put('customfield_11300',case when aMFV_TEILID = 1 then '2936' else '2935'end);
 
  l_json_object.put('components',l_json_array_ak);
 
   l_json_object_fields.put('fields', l_json_object);
 
 l_return:=  replace(l_json_object_fields.to_clob,'\\r\\n','\r\n') ;
    return l_return;
 
 
 
end fCreateJiraUrlAssistent;
 
procedure pAddCocoaAnhangToTicket(AJiraTicket varchar2, aCocoaTicket Varchar2) as
PRAGMA AUTONOMOUS_TRANSACTION;
begin
insert into t_jira_anhang (JIRA_TICKET,ANHANG_NAME,ANHANG_URL, STatus) 
 
Select AJiraTicket,filename,attcontent,0 FROM
                  t_x_cocoa_import t, 
                  JSON_TABLE ( data_clob, '$.fields.attachment[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
 
                               filename VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$.filename',
                              attcontent VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$.content'
                          )
                      )
                  x
                  where t.jira_issue_key = aCocoaTicket;
                  commit;
 
end pAddCocoaAnhangToTicket;
 
 
procedure pAddCocoaInhalttoTicket(AJiraTicket varchar2, aCocoaTicket Varchar2) as
PRAGMA AUTONOMOUS_TRANSACTION;
  l_customfield_53161 CLOB;
    l_customfield_53162 CLOB;
    l_customfield_53163 CLOB;
    l_json_object JSON_OBJECT_T;
    l_json_object_fields JSON_OBJECT_T;
    lreturn clob;
begin
l_json_object := JSON_OBJECT_T();
  l_json_object_fields := JSON_OBJECT_T();
if (aCocoaTicket is not null) 
then
for c in (SELECT
                  x.*,t.*
 
 
              FROM
                  t_x_cocoa_import t, 
                  JSON_TABLE ( data_clob, '$.fields[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
                              --restjson CLOB FORMAT JSON PATH '$',
                               customfield_53161 CLOB  PATH '$.customfield_53161',
                               customfield_53162 CLOB PATH '$.customfield_53162',
                               customfield_53163 CLOB  PATH '$.customfield_53163'
                          )
                      )
                  x where t.jira_issue_key = aCocoaTicket)
loop
l_customfield_53161 := c.customfield_53161;
l_customfield_53162 := c.customfield_53162;
l_customfield_53163 := c.customfield_53163;
end loop;
l_json_object.put('customfield_18417',l_customfield_53161);
l_json_object.put('customfield_18418',l_customfield_53162);
l_json_object.put('customfield_18419',l_customfield_53163);
 
 l_json_object_fields.put('fields', l_json_object);
 lreturn :=  replace(l_json_object_fields.to_clob,'\\r\\n','\r\n') ;
 insert into t_jira_post(JIRA_KEY,POST_CLOB)
values( AJiraTicket,lreturn);
commit;
end if;
 
end pAddCocoaInhalttoTicket;
