-- postNewTicketinQueue
 
FUNCTION postNewTicketinQueue(
    aVorschriftId NUMBER, 
    aMFV_TEILID NUMBER,
    aAKIDS VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    aSchlagwörter VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL, 
    aZusVorschriften VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL, 
    aMFVID VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL, 
    aprevMFVid NUMBER DEFAULT NULL,
    aCocoaTicket VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    aIsClone NUMBER DEFAULT 0,
    aSourceTVRBTicket VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL
) RETURN NUMBER AS
    l_jira_post_id NUMBER;
    l_post_clob CLOB;
BEGIN
    debug('postNewTicketinQueue', '========== START ==========');
    debug('postNewTicketinQueue', 'VorschriftID: ' || aVorschriftId);
    debug('postNewTicketinQueue', 'MfV Teil: ' || aMFV_TEILID);
    debug('postNewTicketinQueue', 'IsClone: ' || aIsClone);
    debug('postNewTicketinQueue', 'SourceTicket: ' || NVL(aSourceTVRBTicket, '[NULL]'));
    
    -- Determine if this is a clone operation
    IF aIsClone = 1 AND aSourceTVRBTicket IS NOT NULL THEN
        debug('postNewTicketinQueue', '>>> CLONE MODE - Using fCloneTicketData');
        
        -- Use cloning function
        l_post_clob := fCloneTicketData(
            aSourceTVRBTicket,
            aVorschriftId,
            aMFV_TEILID,
            aAKIDS,
            aSchlagwörter,
            aZusVorschriften,
            aMFVID,
            aprevMFVid,
            aCocoaTicket
        );
        
        debug('postNewTicketinQueue', 'Clone JSON created - Length: ' || LENGTH(l_post_clob));
        
    ELSE
        debug('postNewTicketinQueue', '>>> NORMAL MODE - Using fCreateJiraUrlAssistent');
        
        -- fCreateJiraUrlAssistent function
        l_post_clob := fCreateJiraUrlAssistent(
            aVorschriftId,
            aMFV_TEILID,
            aAKIDS,
            aSchlagwörter,
            aZusVorschriften,
            aMFVID,
            aprevMFVid,
            aCocoaTicket
        );
        
        debug('postNewTicketinQueue', 'Normal JSON created - Length: ' || LENGTH(l_post_clob));
    END IF;
    
    -- Insert into queue
    INSERT INTO t_jira_post(
        POST_CLOB, 
        COCOA_TICKET,
        IS_CLONE,
        SOURCE_TVRB_TICKET,
        POST_STATUS
        -- ERSTELLUNGS_DATUM
    ) VALUES (
        l_post_clob,
        aCocoaTicket,
        NVL(aIsClone, 0),
        aSourceTVRBTicket,
        0 -- Status: waiting to be processed
        -- SYSDATE
    )
    RETURNING JIRA_POST_ID INTO l_jira_post_id;
    
    debug('postNewTicketinQueue', 'Inserted into T_JIRA_POST - ID: ' || l_jira_post_id);
    debug('postNewTicketinQueue', '========== COMPLETE ==========');
    
    RETURN l_jira_post_id;
    
EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        debug('postNewTicketinQueue', 'FATAL ERROR: ' || SQLERRM);
        debug('postNewTicketinQueue', DBMS_UTILITY.FORMAT_ERROR_BACKTRACE);
        RAISE;
END postNewTicketinQueue;
 
 
 
 
 
procedure pcheckTicketNumberupdate as
begin
 
insert into t_jira_post (JIRA_KEY,POST_CLOB)
WITH cte1 AS (
              SELECT
                  x.*,
                  t_x_mfv_cip.mfv_cipid
 
 
              FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip,
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
                              json VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$',
                              jiraid VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.id', issuetypeid number path '$.fields.issuetype.id',
                              mfv_name VARCHAR2 ( 250 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_11635',
                               jirakey VARCHAR2 ( 32 ) PATH '$.key'
                              )
                          )x 
                           WHERE
                                  substr(jirakey, 0, 4) = gENVIRONMENT and issuetypeid in (13733,14201)
), cte2 as ( Select jirakey,replace(mfv_name , 'TVRB'||'-XXXXX' ,jirakey) as mfv_name_neu,mfv_name
from cte1
where instr(   mfv_name , 'TVRB'||'-XXXXX') > 0
   )             
Select jirakey, json_object ( key 'fields' value
 json_object (key 'customfield_11635' value mfv_name_neu)) as post_clob
 from cte2;
             commit;   
 
end  pcheckTicketNumberupdate;
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
PROCEDURE pAdoptInterpretationMfVs(
    p_new_vorschriftid NUMBER,
    p_mfvid_list VARCHAR2
) AS
    l_jira_key VARCHAR2(100);
    l_current_links CLOB;
    l_new_permalink VARCHAR2(4000);
    l_updated_links CLOB;
    l_json_object JSON_OBJECT_T;
    l_json_fields JSON_OBJECT_T;
    l_post_clob CLOB;
    
BEGIN
    -- Get the new regulation's permalink
    l_new_permalink := PCK_RI.fCreatePermalinkUrl(p_new_vorschriftid);
    
    -- DEBUG: ENABLED
    debug('pAdoptMfVs', 'START - VorschriftID: ' || p_new_vorschriftid);
    debug('pAdoptMfVs', 'MfV List: ' || p_mfvid_list);
    debug('pAdoptMfVs', 'New Permalink: ' || SUBSTR(l_new_permalink, 1, 200));
    
    -- Loop through each selected MFVID
    FOR c IN (
        SELECT COLUMN_VALUE AS mfvid
        FROM TABLE(APEX_STRING.SPLIT_NUMBERS(p_mfvid_list, ':'))
        WHERE COLUMN_VALUE IS NOT NULL
    ) LOOP
        
        BEGIN
            debug('pAdoptMfVs', '>>> Processing MFVID: ' || c.mfvid);
            
            -- 1. CHECK DATABASE 
            DECLARE
                l_already_linked NUMBER;
            BEGIN
                SELECT COUNT(*)
                INTO l_already_linked
                FROM t_mfv_ref_vorschrift
                WHERE mfvid = c.mfvid
                AND vorschriftid = p_new_vorschriftid;
                
                debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    DB Check - Count: ' || l_already_linked);
                
                IF l_already_linked > 0 THEN
                    debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    SKIP: Already linked in database');
                    CONTINUE;
                END IF;
            END;
            
            debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    Not linked yet - continuing...');
            
            -- 2. Get Jira ticket key
            BEGIN
                SELECT jira_ticket 
                INTO l_jira_key
                FROM t_mfv
                WHERE mfvid = c.mfvid;
                
                debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    Jira Ticket: ' || NVL(l_jira_key, '[NULL]'));
            EXCEPTION
                WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
                    debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    ERROR: MFVID not found in T_MFV');
                    CONTINUE;
            END;
            
            -- Skip if no Jira ticket
            IF l_jira_key IS NULL OR TRIM(l_jira_key) = '' THEN
                debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    SKIP: No Jira ticket');
                CONTINUE;
            END IF;
            
            debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    Has Jira ticket - continuing...');
            
            -- 3. Get current customfield_18411 value from cached Jira data
            l_current_links := NULL;
            BEGIN
                SELECT x.vorschriftid
                INTO l_current_links
                FROM t_x_mfv_cip t,
                     JSON_TABLE(mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                         COLUMNS (
                             jirakey VARCHAR2(32) PATH '$.key',
                             vorschriftid CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_18411'
                         )
                     ) x
                WHERE x.jirakey = l_jira_key
                  AND ROWNUM = 1;
                  
                debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    Current Links: ' || NVL(SUBSTR(l_current_links, 1, 100), '[EMPTY]'));
            EXCEPTION
                WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
                    l_current_links := NULL;
                    debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    No cached data in T_X_MFV_CIP');
            END;
            
            -- 4. Check if VorschriftID already exists in Jira
            -- IF l_current_links IS NOT NULL AND 
            --    (INSTR(l_current_links, 'P25_VORSCHRIFTID:' || p_new_vorschriftid) > 0 OR
            --     INSTR(l_current_links, 'P25_VORSCHRIFTID%3A' || p_new_vorschriftid) > 0) THEN
            --     debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    SKIP: VorschriftID already exists in Jira cache');
            --     CONTINUE;
            -- END IF;
 
            -- 4. Check if VorschriftID already exists in Jira 
            IF l_current_links IS NOT NULL THEN
                -- Check for the VorschriftID number pattern
                IF REGEXP_LIKE(l_current_links, '(P25_VORSCHRIFTID:|P25_VORSCHRIFTID%3A)' || p_new_vorschriftid || '($|[^0-9])') THEN
                    debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    SKIP: VorschriftID already exists in Jira cache');
                    CONTINUE;
                END IF;
            END IF;
            
            debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    VorschriftID not in cache - will add');
            
            -- 5. Build updated links string
            IF l_current_links IS NULL OR LENGTH(TRIM(l_current_links)) = 0 THEN
                l_updated_links := l_new_permalink;
                debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    New link (first)');
            ELSE
                l_updated_links := l_current_links || ', ' || l_new_permalink;
                debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    Appended to existing');
            END IF;
            
            debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    Updated links length: ' || LENGTH(l_updated_links));
            
            -- 6. Create JSON payload for Jira REST API
            l_json_object := JSON_OBJECT_T();
            l_json_fields := JSON_OBJECT_T();
            l_json_fields.put('customfield_18411', l_updated_links);
            l_json_object.put('fields', l_json_fields);
            l_post_clob := l_json_object.to_clob();
            
            debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    JSON Length: ' || LENGTH(l_post_clob));
            
            -- 7. Insert into Jira REST API queue
            INSERT INTO t_jira_post (
                JIRA_KEY,
                POST_CLOB,
                POST_STATUS,
                ERSTELLUNGS_DATUM
            ) VALUES (
                l_jira_key,
                l_post_clob,
                0,
                SYSDATE
            );
            
            debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    Inserted into T_JIRA_POST');
            
            -- 8. Link MfV to regulation in database
            INSERT INTO t_mfv_ref_vorschrift (
                mfvid,
                vorschriftid,
                LETZTE_AENDERUNG_DATUM,
                LETZTE_AENDERUNG_BENUTZERID
            ) VALUES (
                c.mfvid,
                p_new_vorschriftid,
                SYSDATE,
                PCK_RI.fGetUserId
            );
            
            debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    Linked in T_MFV_REF_VORSCHRIFT');
            
        EXCEPTION
            WHEN OTHERS THEN
                debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    ERROR for MFVID ' || c.mfvid || ': ' || SQLERRM);
                debug('pAdoptMfVs', '    Backtrace: ' || DBMS_UTILITY.FORMAT_ERROR_BACKTRACE);
                NULL;
        END;
        
    END LOOP;
    
    COMMIT;
    debug('pAdoptMfVs', 'COMPLETE - Committed');
    
EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        ROLLBACK;
        debug('pAdoptMfVs', 'FATAL ERROR: ' || SQLERRM);
        debug('pAdoptMfVs', DBMS_UTILITY.FORMAT_ERROR_BACKTRACE);
        RAISE;
END pAdoptInterpretationMfVs;
 
 
 
-- fCloneTicketData
FUNCTION fCloneTicketData(
    p_source_jira_key VARCHAR2,
    p_new_vorschriftid NUMBER,
    p_mfv_teilid NUMBER,
    p_akids VARCHAR2,
    p_schlagwoerter VARCHAR2,
    p_zusvorschriften VARCHAR2,
    p_mfvid VARCHAR2,
    p_prev_mfvid NUMBER,
    p_cocoa_ticket VARCHAR2
) RETURN CLOB AS
    l_base_json CLOB;
    l_json_object JSON_OBJECT_T;
    l_json_fields JSON_OBJECT_T;
    
    -- Fields to clone from source ticket 
    l_customfield_18417 CLOB;  -- Background for Interpretation / Information
    l_customfield_18418 CLOB;  -- Regulatory background / References
    l_customfield_18419 CLOB;  -- Description / Interpretation
    l_customfield_14505 CLOB;  -- Impact
    l_customfield_18428 CLOB;  -- Affected organisational units
    l_customfield_18420 CLOB;  -- Contributors
    l_customfield_17402 CLOB;  -- Analyse
    l_customfield_18413 CLOB;  -- Beschreibung für Anhänge
    l_customfield_18416 CLOB;  -- Protokoll
    l_description CLOB;        -- Description field
    l_issuelinks CLOB;         -- COCOA Links (issuelinks)
  
BEGIN
    debug('fCloneTicketData', 'START - Source: ' || p_source_jira_key);
    debug('fCloneTicketData', 'VorschriftID: ' || p_new_vorschriftid);
    
    -- 1. Get base ticket JSON using fCreateJiraUrlAssistent function
    l_base_json := fCreateJiraUrlAssistent(
        p_new_vorschriftid,
        p_mfv_teilid,
        p_akids,
        p_schlagwoerter,
        p_zusvorschriften,
        p_mfvid,
        p_prev_mfvid,
        p_cocoa_ticket
    );
    
    debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Base JSON created - Length: ' || LENGTH(l_base_json));
    
    -- 2. Extract cloned fields from source ticket (from T_X_MFV_CIP cache)
    BEGIN
        SELECT 
            x.customfield_18417,
            x.customfield_18418,
            x.customfield_18419,
            x.customfield_14505,
            x.customfield_18428,
            x.customfield_18420,
            x.customfield_17402,
            x.customfield_18413,
            x.customfield_18416,
            x.description,
            x.issuelinks
        INTO 
            l_customfield_18417,
            l_customfield_18418,
            l_customfield_18419,
            l_customfield_14505,
            l_customfield_18428,
            l_customfield_18420,
            l_customfield_17402,
            l_customfield_18413,
            l_customfield_18416,
            l_description,
            l_issuelinks
        FROM t_x_mfv_cip t,
             JSON_TABLE(mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                 COLUMNS (
                     jirakey VARCHAR2(32) PATH '$.key',
                     customfield_18417 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_18417',
                     customfield_18418 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_18418',
                     customfield_18419 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_18419',
                     customfield_14505 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_14505',
                     customfield_18428 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_18428',
                     customfield_18420 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_18420',
                     customfield_17402 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_17402',
                     customfield_18413 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_18413',
                     customfield_18416 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_18416',
                     description CLOB PATH '$.fields.description',
                     issuelinks CLOB PATH '$.fields.issuelinks'
                 )
             ) x
        WHERE x.jirakey = p_source_jira_key
          AND ROWNUM = 1;
          
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Extracted fields from source ticket');
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Background (18417) length: ' || NVL(LENGTH(l_customfield_18417), 0));
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Regulatory background (18418) length: ' || NVL(LENGTH(l_customfield_18418), 0));
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Description (18419) length: ' || NVL(LENGTH(l_customfield_18419), 0));
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Impact (14505) length: ' || NVL(LENGTH(l_customfield_14505), 0));
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Affected units (18428) length: ' || NVL(LENGTH(l_customfield_18428), 0));
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Contributors (18420) length: ' || NVL(LENGTH(l_customfield_18420), 0));
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Analyse (17402) length: ' || NVL(LENGTH(l_customfield_17402), 0));
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Beschreibung Anhänge (18413) length: ' || NVL(LENGTH(l_customfield_18413), 0));
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Protokoll (18416) length: ' || NVL(LENGTH(l_customfield_18416), 0));
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Description length: ' || NVL(LENGTH(l_description), 0));
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Issuelinks length: ' || NVL(LENGTH(l_issuelinks), 0));
        
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
            debug('fCloneTicketData', 'WARNING: Source ticket not found in T_X_MFV_CIP cache');
            -- Continue with empty fields
            l_customfield_18417 := NULL;
            l_customfield_18418 := NULL;
            l_customfield_18419 := NULL;
            l_customfield_14505 := NULL;
            l_customfield_18428 := NULL;
            l_customfield_18420 := NULL;
            l_customfield_17402 := NULL;
            l_customfield_18413 := NULL;
            l_customfield_18416 := NULL;
            l_description := NULL;
            l_issuelinks := NULL;
    END;
    
    -- 3. Parse base JSON and add cloned fields
    l_json_object := JSON_OBJECT_T.parse(l_base_json);
    l_json_fields := JSON_OBJECT_T(l_json_object.get('fields'));
    
    debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Parsed JSON - Adding cloned fields...');
    
    -- cloned work results
    IF l_customfield_18417 IS NOT NULL THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_18417', l_customfield_18417);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Added Background for Interpretation (18417)');
    END IF;
    
    IF l_customfield_18418 IS NOT NULL THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_18418', l_customfield_18418);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Added Regulatory background (18418)');
    END IF;
    
    IF l_customfield_18419 IS NOT NULL THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_18419', l_customfield_18419);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Added Description/Interpretation (18419)');
    END IF;
    
    IF l_customfield_14505 IS NOT NULL THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_14505', l_customfield_14505);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Added Impact (14505)');
    END IF;
    
    IF l_customfield_18428 IS NOT NULL THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_18428', l_customfield_18428);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Added Affected organisational units (18428)');
    END IF;
    
    IF l_customfield_18420 IS NOT NULL THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_18420', l_customfield_18420);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Added Contributors (18420)');
    END IF;
    
    IF l_customfield_17402 IS NOT NULL THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_17402', l_customfield_17402);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Added Analyse (17402)');
    END IF;
    
    IF l_customfield_18413 IS NOT NULL THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_18413', l_customfield_18413);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Added Beschreibung für Anhänge (18413)');
    END IF;
    
    IF l_customfield_18416 IS NOT NULL THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_18416', l_customfield_18416);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Added Protokoll (18416)');
    END IF;
    
    -- Description field
    IF l_description IS NOT NULL THEN
        l_json_fields.put('description', l_description);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Added Description');
    END IF;
    
    -- COCOA Links (issuelinks)
    IF l_issuelinks IS NOT NULL THEN
        l_json_fields.put('issuelinks', l_issuelinks);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'Added Issuelinks');
    END IF;
    
    -- Update the fields object
    l_json_object.put('fields', l_json_fields);
    
    debug('fCloneTicketData', 'COMPLETE - Final JSON length: ' || LENGTH(l_json_object.to_clob()));
    
    RETURN l_json_object.to_clob();
    
EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        debug('fCloneTicketData', 'ERROR: ' || SQLERRM);
        debug('fCloneTicketData', DBMS_UTILITY.FORMAT_ERROR_BACKTRACE);
        RAISE;
END fCloneTicketData;
 
 
 
-- pCloneAttachments
 
PROCEDURE pCloneAttachments(
    p_source_jira_key VARCHAR2,
    p_target_jira_key VARCHAR2
) AS
    PRAGMA AUTONOMOUS_TRANSACTION;
    l_count NUMBER := 0;
BEGIN
    debug('pCloneAttachments', 'START - Source: ' || p_source_jira_key);
    debug('pCloneAttachments', 'Target: ' || p_target_jira_key);
    
    -- Copy attachments from source ticket
 
    insert into t_jira_anhang(JIRA_TICKET,ANHANG_NAME,ANHANG_URL, STatus) 
 
           Select p_target_jira_key,filename,attcontent,0 FROM
                  t_x_mfv_cip t, 
                  JSON_TABLE ( mfv_data_clob,  '$.fields.attachment[*]'
                          COLUMNS (
 
                               filename VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$.filename',
                              attcontent VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$.content'
                          )
                      )
                  x
                  where t.jira_key = p_source_jira_key;
                 
    
 
    
    l_count := SQL%ROWCOUNT;
    
    debug('pCloneAttachments', 'Copied ' || l_count || ' attachments');
    
    COMMIT;
    
EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        ROLLBACK;
        debug('pCloneAttachments', 'ERROR: ' || SQLERRM);
        debug('pCloneAttachments', DBMS_UTILITY.FORMAT_ERROR_BACKTRACE);
        RAISE;
END pCloneAttachments;
 
 
--Main Update Procedure
PROCEDURE pUpdateOpenTickets(
    p_vorschriftid NUMBER
) AS
BEGIN
    debug('pUpdateOpenTickets', '========== START ==========');
    debug('pUpdateOpenTickets', 'VorschriftID: ' || p_vorschriftid);
    
    -- Loop through all open MfVs linked to this VorschriftID
    FOR rec IN (
        SELECT DISTINCT tm.mfvid, tm.jira_ticket
        FROM t_mfv tm
        JOIN t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv ON tm.mfvid = tmrv.mfvid
        WHERE (
            -- Main regulation
            tmrv.vorschriftid = p_vorschriftid
            -- OR consolidated regulations (beziehung_art = 200)
            OR tmrv.vorschriftid IN (
                SELECT vorgaenger_vorschriftid 
                FROM t_vorschrift_ref_vorschrift 
                WHERE nachfolger_vorschriftid = p_vorschriftid 
                  AND beziehung_art = 200
            )
        )
        AND tm.jira_status = 0  -- Open only (0 = offen)
        AND tm.jira_ticket IS NOT NULL
        ORDER BY tm.mfvid
    ) LOOP
        debug('pUpdateOpenTickets', '>>> Processing MFVID: ' || rec.mfvid || ' | Ticket: ' || rec.jira_ticket);
        
        BEGIN
            -- Update this ticket
            pUpdateMfVTicket(rec.mfvid);
        EXCEPTION
            WHEN OTHERS THEN
                debug('pUpdateOpenTickets', 'ERROR for MFVID ' || rec.mfvid || ': ' || SQLERRM);
                -- Continue with next ticket
        END;
    END LOOP;
    
    COMMIT;
    debug('pUpdateOpenTickets', '========== COMPLETE ==========');
    
EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        ROLLBACK;
        debug('pUpdateOpenTickets', 'FATAL ERROR: ' || SQLERRM);
        debug('pUpdateOpenTickets', DBMS_UTILITY.FORMAT_ERROR_BACKTRACE);
        RAISE;
END pUpdateOpenTickets;
 
 
-- Update Individual Ticket
 
PROCEDURE pUpdateMfVTicket(
    p_mfvid NUMBER
) AS
    l_jira_ticket VARCHAR2(100);
    l_has_changes BOOLEAN := FALSE;
    l_json_object JSON_OBJECT_T;
    l_json_fields JSON_OBJECT_T;
    
    -- Current JIRA values (from T_X_MFV_CIP cache)
    l_curr_components CLOB;
    l_curr_18422 CLOB;
    l_curr_10302 CLOB;
    l_curr_19400 CLOB;
    l_curr_18402 CLOB;
    l_curr_19317 VARCHAR2(100);
    l_curr_18301 CLOB;
    l_curr_11643 VARCHAR2(250);
    l_curr_16524 CLOB;
    l_curr_19000 CLOB;
    l_curr_19700 clob;
    l_curr_18411 VARCHAR2(100);
    l_main_vorschriftid number;
    -- New RegIndex values
    l_new_components CLOB;
    l_new_18422 CLOB;
    l_new_10302 CLOB;
    l_new_19400 CLOB;
    l_new_18402 CLOB;
    l_new_19317 VARCHAR2(100);
    l_new_18301 CLOB;
    l_new_11643 VARCHAR2(250);
    l_new_16524 CLOB;
    l_new_19700 CLOB;
    l_new_19000 CLOB;
    -- Temp variables
    l_json_array JSON_ARRAY_T;
    l_json_obj JSON_OBJECT_T;
    l_temp CLOB;
    
BEGIN
    debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '========== START ==========');
    debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'MFVID: ' || p_mfvid);
    
    -- 1. Get JIRA ticket key
    BEGIN
        SELECT jira_ticket INTO l_jira_ticket
        FROM t_mfv WHERE mfvid = p_mfvid;
        
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'Ticket: ' || l_jira_ticket);
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'ERROR: MFVID not found');
            RETURN;
    END;
    
    -- 2. Get CURRENT JIRA values from cache
    BEGIN
        SELECT 
            x.components,
            x.customfield_18422,
            x.customfield_10302,
            x.customfield_19400,
            x.customfield_18402,
            x.customfield_19317,
            x.customfield_18301,
            x.customfield_11643,
            x.customfield_16524,
            case when instr(x.customfield_18411, ',') > 0 then
           substr(x.customfield_18411,instr(x.customfield_18411, 'VORSCHRIFTID:')+13, instr(x.customfield_18411, ',')-(instr(x.customfield_18411, 'VORSCHRIFTID:')+13))
           else
           substr(x.customfield_18411,instr(x.customfield_18411, 'VORSCHRIFTID:')+13)
           end,
           x.customfield_19700
        INTO 
            l_curr_components,
            l_curr_18422,
            l_curr_10302,
            l_curr_19400,
            l_curr_18402,
            l_curr_19317,
            l_curr_18301,
            l_curr_11643,
            l_curr_16524,
            l_curr_18411,
            l_curr_19700
        FROM t_x_mfv_cip t,
             JSON_TABLE(mfv_data_clob, '$[*]'
                 COLUMNS (
                     jirakey VARCHAR2(32) PATH '$.key',
                     components CLOB PATH '$.fields.components',
                     customfield_18422 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_18422',
                     customfield_10302 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_10302',
                     customfield_19400 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_19400',
                     customfield_18402 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_18402',
                     customfield_19317 VARCHAR2(100) PATH '$.fields.customfield_19317.value',
                     customfield_18301 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_18301',
                     customfield_11643 VARCHAR2(250) PATH '$.fields.customfield_11643',
                     customfield_16524 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_16524',
                     customfield_18411 VARCHAR2 ( 4000 ) PATH '$.fields.customfield_18411',
                     customfield_19700 CLOB PATH '$.fields.customfield_197000'
                 )
             ) x
        WHERE t.jira_key = l_jira_ticket
          AND ROWNUM = 1;
        -- Berechnen der Main Vorschrift
    l_main_vorschriftid := cast(l_curr_18411 as number);  
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'Current JIRA data retrieved');
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'WARNING: No cached JIRA data found - skipping');
            RETURN;
    END;
    
    
    -- 3. BUILD NEW REGINDEX VALUES
 
    debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'Building new RegIndex values...');
    
    -- FIELD 1: Components (Arbeitskreise)
 
    BEGIN
        l_json_array := JSON_ARRAY_T();
        
        FOR rec IN (
            SELECT DISTINCT a.jiraid, a.kurz
            FROM t_mfv_ref_et_b_ak tmra
            JOIN t_et_b_ak a ON tmra.et_b_akid = a.et_b_akid
            WHERE tmra.mfvid = p_mfvid
            ORDER BY a.kurz  -- Order by the selected column
        ) LOOP
            l_json_obj := JSON_OBJECT_T();
            l_json_obj.put('id', rec.jiraid);
            l_json_array.append(l_json_obj);
        END LOOP;
        
        -- Convert to CLOB
        IF l_json_array.get_size() > 0 THEN
            l_new_components := l_json_array.to_clob();
        ELSE
            l_new_components := '[]';  -- Empty array as string
        END IF;
        
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '1. Components: ' || LENGTH(NVL(l_new_components, ' ')) || ' chars');
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            l_new_components := '[]';
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '1. Components: ERROR - ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
 
    -- FIELD 2: Predecessor Regulations (18422)
    
    BEGIN
        SELECT LISTAGG(tv.vorschrift_nummer, ', ') WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY tv.vorschrift_nummer)
        INTO l_new_18422
        FROM t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv
        JOIN t_vorschrift tv ON tmrv.vorschriftid = tv.vorschriftid
        JOIN t_vorschrift_ref_vorschrift tvrv ON tv.vorschriftid = tvrv.nachfolger_vorschriftid
        JOIN t_vorschrift tvp ON tvrv.vorgaenger_vorschriftid = tvp.vorschriftid
        WHERE tmrv.mfvid = p_mfvid
          AND tvrv.beziehung_art = 10 and tmrv.vorschriftid = l_main_vorschriftid;
          
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '2. Predecessor: ' || NVL(SUBSTR(l_new_18422, 1, 50), '[EMPTY]'));
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
            l_new_18422 := NULL;
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '2. Predecessor: [EMPTY]');
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            l_new_18422 := NULL;
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '2. Predecessor: ERROR - ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    
    -- FIELD 3: Application Dates (10302) - MULTI-REGULATION
    
    BEGIN
        l_new_10302 := NULL;
        l_temp := NULL;
        
        FOR rec IN (
            SELECT 
                tmrv.vorschriftid,
                tv.vorschrift_nummer,
                ROW_NUMBER() over( ORDER BY case when tmrv.vorschriftid = l_main_vorschriftid then 0 else 1 end,  tv.vorschrift_nummer) sort_order
            FROM t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv
            JOIN t_vorschrift tv ON tmrv.vorschriftid = tv.vorschriftid
            WHERE tmrv.mfvid = p_mfvid 
             -- Main first!
        ) LOOP
            DECLARE
                l_dates CLOB;
            BEGIN
                SELECT LISTAGG(
                    edt.einsatzdatum_typ || ': ' || 
                    CASE 
                        WHEN vre.einsatzdatum_typid IN (1030, 1031) AND vre.modeljahr IS NOT NULL 
                        THEN 'Modelljahr ' || TO_CHAR(vre.modeljahr, 'YYYY')
                        ELSE TO_CHAR(vre.einsatzdatum, 'DD.MM.YYYY')
                    END,
                    ',' || CHR(13) || CHR(10)
                ) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY edt.sortorder)
                INTO l_dates
                FROM t_vorschrift_ref_einsatzdatum_typ vre
                JOIN t_einsatzdatum_typ edt ON vre.einsatzdatum_typid = edt.einsatzdatum_typid
                WHERE vre.vorschriftid = rec.vorschriftid
                  AND vre.einsatzdatum IS NOT NULL
                  AND vre.einsatzdatum_typid NOT IN (1031) and (FAHRZEUGKLASSEID is null or FAHRZEUGKLASSEID = 1024);
                
                IF l_dates IS NOT NULL THEN
                    IF rec.sort_order = 1 THEN
                        -- Main regulation
                        l_new_10302 := 'Application timing main regulation: ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || l_dates;
                    ELSE
                        -- Additional regulation
                        IF l_temp IS NULL THEN
                            l_temp := CHR(13) || CHR(10) || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || 
                                     'Application timing additional regulation(s): ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10);
                        END IF;
                        l_temp := l_temp || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || 
                                 rec.vorschrift_nummer || ': ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || l_dates;
                    END IF;
                END IF;
            EXCEPTION
                WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
                    NULL;
            END;
        END LOOP;
        
        l_new_10302 := l_new_10302 || NVL(l_temp, '');
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '3. Application Dates: ' || LENGTH(NVL(l_new_10302, ' ')) || ' chars');
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            l_new_10302 := NULL;
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '3. Application Dates: ERROR - ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
 
    -- FIELD 4: Themes (19400)
    
    BEGIN
        SELECT LISTAGG(DISTINCT tt.bezeichnung, ', ') WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY tt.bezeichnung)
        INTO l_new_19400
        FROM t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv
        JOIN t_vorschrift_ref_thema tvrt ON tmrv.vorschriftid = tvrt.vorschriftid
        JOIN t_thema tt ON tvrt.themaid = tt.themaid
        WHERE tmrv.mfvid = p_mfvid and tmrv.vorschriftid = l_main_vorschriftid
          AND tvrt.geloescht = 0;
          
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '4. Themes: ' || NVL(SUBSTR(l_new_19400, 1, 50), '[EMPTY]'));
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
            l_new_19400 := NULL;
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '4. Themes: [EMPTY]');
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            l_new_19400 := NULL;
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '4. Themes: ERROR - ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
 
    
    -- FIELD 5: Countries (18402)
 
    BEGIN
        l_json_array := JSON_ARRAY_T();
        
        FOR rec IN (
            SELECT DISTINCT cast(tl.jira_code2  as varchar2(50)) jira_code2 
            FROM t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv
            JOIN t_vorschrift_ref_land tvrl ON tmrv.vorschriftid = tvrl.vorschriftid
            JOIN t_land tl ON tvrl.landid = tl.landid
            WHERE tmrv.mfvid = p_mfvid
              AND tvrl.geloescht = 0
              AND tl.jira_code2 IS NOT NULL
            ORDER BY tl.jira_code2
        ) LOOP
            l_json_obj := JSON_OBJECT_T();
            l_json_obj.put('id', rec.jira_code2);
            l_json_array.append(l_json_obj);
        END LOOP;
        
        -- Convert to CLOB
        IF l_json_array.get_size() > 0 THEN
            l_new_18402 := l_json_array.to_clob();
        ELSE
            l_new_18402 := '[]';  -- Empty array as string
        END IF;
        
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '5. Countries: ' || LENGTH(NVL(l_new_18402, ' ')) || ' chars');
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            l_new_18402 := '[]';
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '5. Countries: ERROR - ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
 
    -- FIELD 6: SUMS Relevant (19317)
    
    BEGIN
        DECLARE
            v_rxswin NUMBER;
            v_homolog NUMBER;
            v_sums_land NUMBER := 0;
            v_vorschrift_nummer VARCHAR2(250);
        BEGIN
            -- Get first linked Vorschrift data
            SELECT 
                tv.rxswin,
                tv.homologationsrelevant,
                tv.vorschrift_nummer
            INTO 
                v_rxswin,
                v_homolog,
                v_vorschrift_nummer
            FROM t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv
            JOIN t_vorschrift tv ON tmrv.vorschriftid = tv.vorschriftid
            WHERE tmrv.mfvid = p_mfvid and tmrv.vorschriftid = l_main_vorschriftid
              AND ROWNUM = 1
            ORDER BY tmrv.mfv_ref_vorschriftid;
            
            -- Check if has SUMS relevant countries
            BEGIN
                SELECT COUNT(*)
                INTO v_sums_land
                FROM t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv
                JOIN t_vorschrift_ref_land tvrl ON tmrv.vorschriftid = tvrl.vorschriftid
                JOIN t_land tl ON tvrl.landid = tl.landid
                WHERE tmrv.mfvid = p_mfvid and tmrv.vorschriftid = l_main_vorschriftid
                  AND tl.sums_relevant = 10
                  AND ROWNUM = 1;
            EXCEPTION
                WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
                    v_sums_land := 0;
            END;
            
            -- Determine SUMS value
            IF v_rxswin = 10 AND v_homolog = 10 AND (v_sums_land = 1 OR SUBSTR(v_vorschrift_nummer, 1, 4) = 'UN-R') THEN
                l_new_19317 := '54882';  -- Yes
            ELSIF v_rxswin = 0 AND v_homolog = 10 THEN
                l_new_19317 := '54881';  -- No
            ELSIF v_rxswin = 20 AND v_homolog = 10 AND (v_sums_land = 1 OR SUBSTR(v_vorschrift_nummer, 1, 4) = 'UN-R') THEN
                l_new_19317 := '63464';  -- Not rated
            ELSE
                l_new_19317 := '54881';  -- No (default)
            END IF;
            
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '6. SUMS Relevant: ' || l_new_19317);
        END;
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            l_new_19317 := '54881';  -- Default to No
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '6. SUMS Relevant: ERROR - ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
 
    -- FIELD 7: Regulation Number (18301) - MULTI-REGULATION
    
    BEGIN
        l_new_18301 := NULL;
        l_temp := NULL;
        
        FOR rec IN (
            SELECT 
                tv.vorschrift_nummer,
                ROW_NUMBER() over( ORDER BY case when tmrv.vorschriftid = l_main_vorschriftid then 0 else 1 end,  tv.vorschrift_nummer) sort_order
            FROM t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv
            JOIN t_vorschrift tv ON tmrv.vorschriftid = tv.vorschriftid
            WHERE tmrv.mfvid = p_mfvid
           -- Main first!
        ) LOOP
            IF rec.sort_order = 1 THEN
                -- Main regulation
                l_new_18301 := 'Main regulation number: ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || ' ' || rec.vorschrift_nummer;
            ELSE
                -- Additional regulations
                IF l_temp IS NULL THEN
                    l_temp := CHR(13) || CHR(10) || ' ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || 
                             'Additional regulation number(s): ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || ' ';
                ELSE
                    l_temp := l_temp || ', ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || ' ';
                END IF;
                l_temp := l_temp || rec.vorschrift_nummer;
            END IF;
        END LOOP;
        
        l_new_18301 := l_new_18301 || NVL(l_temp, '');
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '7. Reg Number: ' || LENGTH(NVL(l_new_18301, ' ')) || ' chars');
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            l_new_18301 := NULL;
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '7. Reg Number: ERROR - ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
 
    -- FIELD 8: Regulation Title (11643)
    
    BEGIN
        SELECT 
            CASE 
                WHEN LENGTH(tv.vorschrift_bezeichnung) >= 250 
                THEN SUBSTR(tv.vorschrift_bezeichnung, 1, 245) || '...'
                ELSE tv.vorschrift_bezeichnung
            END
        INTO l_new_11643
        FROM t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv
        JOIN t_vorschrift tv ON tmrv.vorschriftid = tv.vorschriftid
        WHERE tmrv.mfvid = p_mfvid and tmrv.vorschriftid = l_main_vorschriftid
          AND ROWNUM = 1
        ORDER BY tmrv.mfv_ref_vorschriftid;  -- Main regulation
        
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '8. Reg Title: ' || NVL(SUBSTR(l_new_11643, 1, 50), '[EMPTY]'));
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN NO_DATA_FOUND THEN
            l_new_11643 := NULL;
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '8. Reg Title: [EMPTY]');
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            l_new_11643 := NULL;
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '8. Reg Title: ERROR - ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
 
    -- FIELD 9: Getex URL (16524) - MULTI-REGULATION
    
    BEGIN
        l_new_16524 := NULL;
        l_temp := NULL;
        
        FOR rec IN (
            SELECT 
                tv.vorschrift_nummer,
                tv.url_getex_vorschrift,
               ROW_NUMBER() over( ORDER BY case when tmrv.vorschriftid = l_main_vorschriftid then 0 else 1 end,  tv.vorschrift_nummer) sort_order
            FROM t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv
            JOIN t_vorschrift tv ON tmrv.vorschriftid = tv.vorschriftid
            WHERE tmrv.mfvid = p_mfvid
           
        ) LOOP
            IF rec.url_getex_vorschrift IS NOT NULL THEN
                IF rec.sort_order = 1 THEN
                    -- Main regulation
                    l_new_16524 := 'Main regulation: ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || 
                                  rec.url_getex_vorschrift || CHR(13) || CHR(10);
                ELSE
                    -- Additional regulation
                    IF l_temp IS NULL THEN
                        l_temp := ' ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || 
                                 'Additional Regulations: ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10);
                    END IF;
                    l_temp := l_temp || rec.vorschrift_nummer || ': ' || 
                             rec.url_getex_vorschrift || ' ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10);
                END IF;
            END IF;
        END LOOP;
        
        l_new_16524 := l_new_16524 || NVL(l_temp, '');
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '9. Getex URL: ' || LENGTH(NVL(l_new_16524, ' ')) || ' chars');
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            l_new_16524 := NULL;
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '9. Getex URL: ERROR - ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    -- Field 10 Status der Vorschrift
     BEGIN
        l_new_19700 := NULL;
        l_temp := NULL;
        
        FOR rec IN (
            SELECT 
                tv.vorschrift_nummer,
                s.status,
               ROW_NUMBER() over( ORDER BY case when tmrv.vorschriftid = l_main_vorschriftid then 0 else 1 end,  tv.vorschrift_nummer) sort_order
            FROM t_mfv_ref_vorschrift tmrv
            JOIN t_vorschrift tv ON tmrv.vorschriftid = tv.vorschriftid
            left outer join t_vorschrift_status s on s.VORSCHRIFT_STATUSID = tv.VORSCHRIFT_STATUSID
            WHERE tmrv.mfvid = p_mfvid
           
        ) LOOP
            IF  rec.status IS NOT NULL THEN
                IF rec.sort_order = 1 THEN
                    -- Main regulation
                    l_new_19700 := 'Status main regulation: ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || 
                                  rec.status || CHR(13) || CHR(10);
                ELSE
                    -- Additional regulation
                    IF l_temp IS NULL THEN
                        l_temp := ' ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10) || 
                                 'Status additional regulation(s): ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10);
                    END IF;
                    l_temp := l_temp || rec.vorschrift_nummer || ': ' || 
                             rec.status || ' ' || CHR(13) || CHR(10);
                END IF;
            END IF;
        END LOOP;
        
        l_new_19700 := l_new_19700 || NVL(l_temp, '');
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '10 Status Vorschrift: ' || LENGTH(NVL(l_new_16524, ' ')) || ' chars');
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            l_new_19700 := NULL;
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '10 Status Vorschrift : ERROR - ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    -- 4. COMPARE AND BUILD JSON FOR CHANGED FIELDS ONLY
 
    debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'Comparing current vs new values...');
 
    l_json_object := JSON_OBJECT_T();
    l_json_fields := JSON_OBJECT_T();
 
    -- Compare Components (stored as CLOB string of JSON array)
    IF NVL(l_curr_components, '[]') != NVL(l_new_components, '[]') THEN
        -- Parse the CLOB string back to JSON array
        IF l_new_components IS NOT NULL AND l_new_components != '[]' THEN
            BEGIN
                l_json_array := JSON_ARRAY_T.parse(l_new_components);
                l_json_fields.put('components', l_json_array);
            EXCEPTION
                WHEN OTHERS THEN
                    debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'ERROR parsing components JSON: ' || SQLERRM);
                    l_json_fields.put('components', JSON_ARRAY_T());
            END;
        ELSE
            l_json_fields.put('components', JSON_ARRAY_T());
        END IF;
        l_has_changes := TRUE;
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'CHANGE DETECTED: Components');
    END IF;
 
    -- Compare Predecessor (string field)
    IF NVL(l_curr_18422, ' ') != NVL(l_new_18422, ' ') THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_18422', NVL(l_new_18422, ''));
        l_has_changes := TRUE;
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'CHANGE DETECTED: Predecessor');
    END IF;
 
    -- Compare Application Dates (string field)
    IF NVL(l_curr_10302, ' ') != NVL(l_new_10302, ' ') THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_10302', NVL(l_new_10302, ''));
        l_has_changes := TRUE;
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'CHANGE DETECTED: Application Dates');
    END IF;
 
    -- Compare Themes (string field)
    IF NVL(l_curr_19400, ' ') != NVL(l_new_19400, ' ') THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_19400', NVL(l_new_19400, ''));
        l_has_changes := TRUE;
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'CHANGE DETECTED: Themes');
    END IF;
 
    -- Compare Countries (stored as CLOB string of JSON array)
    IF NVL(l_curr_18402, '[]') != NVL(l_new_18402, '[]') THEN
        -- Parse the CLOB string back to JSON array
        IF l_new_18402 IS NOT NULL AND l_new_18402 != '[]' THEN
            BEGIN
                l_json_array := JSON_ARRAY_T.parse(l_new_18402);
                l_json_fields.put('customfield_18402', l_json_array);
            EXCEPTION
                WHEN OTHERS THEN
                    debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'ERROR parsing countries JSON: ' || SQLERRM);
                    l_json_fields.put('customfield_18402', JSON_ARRAY_T());
            END;
        ELSE
            l_json_fields.put('customfield_18402', JSON_ARRAY_T());
        END IF;
        l_has_changes := TRUE;
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'CHANGE DETECTED: Countries');
    END IF;
 
    -- Compare SUMS Relevant (object field)
    IF NVL(l_curr_19317, ' ') != NVL(l_new_19317, ' ') THEN
        l_json_obj := JSON_OBJECT_T();
        l_json_obj.put('id', l_new_19317);
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_19317', l_json_obj);
        l_has_changes := TRUE;
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'CHANGE DETECTED: SUMS Relevant');
    END IF;
 
    -- Compare Reg Number (string field)
    IF NVL(l_curr_18301, ' ') != NVL(l_new_18301, ' ') THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_18301', NVL(l_new_18301, ''));
        l_has_changes := TRUE;
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'CHANGE DETECTED: Reg Number');
    END IF;
 
    -- Compare Reg Title (string field)
    IF NVL(l_curr_11643, ' ') != NVL(l_new_11643, ' ') THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_11643', NVL(l_new_11643, ''));
        l_has_changes := TRUE;
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'CHANGE DETECTED: Reg Title');
    END IF;
 
    -- Compare Getex URL (string field)
    IF NVL(l_curr_16524, ' ') != NVL(l_new_16524, ' ') THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_16524', NVL(l_new_16524, ''));
        l_has_changes := TRUE;
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'CHANGE DETECTED: Getex URL');
    END IF;
    
    -- Compare Status
    IF NVL(l_curr_19700, ' ') != NVL(l_new_19700, ' ') THEN
        l_json_fields.put('customfield_19700', NVL(l_new_19700, ''));
        l_has_changes := TRUE;
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'CHANGE DETECTED: Status');
    END IF;
   
-- 5. INSERT INTO QUEUE IF CHANGES FOUND
 
 
IF l_has_changes THEN
    -- Build final JSON object
    l_json_object := JSON_OBJECT_T();
    l_json_object.put('fields', l_json_fields);
    
    -- Convert to CLOB for insert
    DECLARE
        l_final_json CLOB;
    BEGIN
        l_final_json := l_json_object.to_clob();
        
        INSERT INTO t_jira_post (
            JIRA_KEY,
            POST_CLOB,
            POST_STATUS,
            ERSTELLUNGS_DATUM
        ) VALUES (
            l_jira_ticket,
            l_final_json,
            0,  -- Waiting to be processed
            SYSDATE
        );
        
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'UPDATE QUEUED - Changes detected and queued for: ' || l_jira_ticket);
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'JSON Size: ' || LENGTH(l_final_json) || ' chars');
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'ERROR inserting into T_JIRA_POST: ' || SQLERRM);
            RAISE;
    END;
ELSE
    debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'NO CHANGES - Ticket skipped (all fields identical)');
END IF;
 
debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', '========== COMPLETE ==========');
    
EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', 'ERROR: ' || SQLERRM);
        debug('pUpdateMfVTicket', DBMS_UTILITY.FORMAT_ERROR_BACKTRACE);
        RAISE;
END pUpdateMfVTicket;
 
end PCK_CIP_JIRA;
/





================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================================



create or replace PACKAGE "PCK_REV" AS 
    function fCreateRevControlUrl(aVerantwortlicherId NUMBER, aTrackingCode VARCHAR2) return VARCHAR2;
    function fIsAuthorized(aVerantwortlicherid in number, aWert_Hash in varchar2) return BOOLEAN;
    procedure pSendMail(pSubject in varchar2, pBody in nvarchar2, pRcptString in varchar2, pPriority in number);
    procedure pErstelleKontrollGruppe(aName in varchar2, aListeREV in varchar2);

    function fCreateMailLink(aRevKontrollID in number) return varchar2;

    -- function fCreateMailLink(aRevKontrollID number) return varchar2;
    function fCreateMailContent(aRevKontrollID in number) return varchar2;

    -- Send emails
    procedure pSendRevMail(aRevKontrollID in number);

    procedure pConfirmChanges(aRevKontrolleVorschriftID in number);    
END PCK_REV;
/


create or replace PACKAGE BODY "PCK_REV" AS
     function fCreateRevControlUrl(aVerantwortlicherId NUMBER, aTrackingCode VARCHAR2) return varchar2 IS
    BEGIN
        return apex_util.host_url('SCRIPT') || APEX_UTIL.PREPARE_URL(apex_page.get_url(
        p_application => V('APP_ALIAS')
        , p_page => 'REV'
        , p_session => null
        , p_clear_cache => '421'
        , p_items => 'P421_VERANTWORTLICHERID,P421_READ_TRACKING_CODE'
        , p_values => aVerantwortlicherId|| ',' || apex_util.url_encode(aTrackingCode))
        );
    END fCreateRevControlUrl;

    function fIsAuthorized(aVerantwortlicherid in number, aWert_Hash in varchar2) return BOOLEAN is
    lResult NUMBER;
    BEGIN
        select count(verantwortlicherid) into lResult from T_REV_KONTROLLE where verantwortlicherid = aVerantwortlicherid and wert_hash like aWert_Hash;
        RETURN lResult > 0;
    END fIsAuthorized;

    procedure pErstelleKontrollGruppe(aName in varchar2, aListeREV in varchar2) is
        lGruppeID number;
        lRevKontrolleId number;
    begin

        insert into t_rev_kontrolle_gruppe (gruppe_name) values (aName) returning rev_kontrolle_gruppe_id into lGruppeID;

        for x in (select column_value as rev from apex_string.split_numbers(aListeREV,':')) loop
            insert into t_rev_kontrolle (
                verantwortlicherid, rev_kontrolle_gruppe_id
            ) values (
                x.rev, lGruppeId
            ) returning rev_kontrolle_id into lRevKontrolleId;
            update t_rev_kontrolle set wert_hash = standard_hash(rev_kontrolle_id) where rev_kontrolle_id = lRevKontrolleId;

            insert into t_rev_kontrolle_vorschrift (rev_kontrolle_id, vorschriftid)
            select lRevKontrolleId, vorschriftid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_verantwortlicher
            where verantwortlicherid = x.rev;

        end loop;


    end pErstelleKontrollGruppe;

    function fEncode(aString in varchar2) return varchar2 is
    begin

        return apex_escape.html(replace(replace(apex_util.url_encode(aString),'+','%20'),chr(10),'%0D'));    

    end fEncode;

    -- It will show preview before Sending emails Directly

    function fCreateMailLink(aRevKontrollID number) return varchar2 is
        lMailLink varchar2(4000 char); 
        cSubject constant varchar2(2000 char) := 'Bitte prüfen Sie Ihre Regulierungsverantwortlichkeiten';
        -- / Please check your regulatory responsibilities
        lBody_DE varchar2(2000 char);   -- German
        -- lBody_EN varchar2(2000 char);   -- English
        lBody varchar2(4000 char);      -- Final combined body
    begin
        for x in (
            select k.verantwortlicherid, k.wert_hash, v.email, v.vorname, v.nachname
            from t_rev_kontrolle k
            join t_verantwortlicher v on (k.verantwortlicherid = v.verantwortlicherid)
            where k.rev_kontrolle_id = aRevKontrollID
        ) loop
            -- German Text
            lBody_DE := 'Sehr geehrte/r ' || x.vorname || ' ' || x.nachname || ',' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Im Prozess XYZ ist festgelegt, dass quartalsweise die Richtigkeit der Daten vom Regulierungsverantwortlichen bestätigt werden muss.' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Bitte bestätigen Sie, dass Sie im System ET-B Regulation Index für eine oder mehrere fahrzeugtechnische Vorschriften als Regulierungsverantwortlicher (REV) genannt sind.' || chr(10) || 
                'Klicken Sie bitte auf den Link, um zu einer Maske weitergeleitet zu werden, in der Sie sehen können, für welche Vorschriften Sie als REV eingetragen sind.' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Hilfestellungen zum System finden Sie direkt in der Maske über die ? Icons!' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                '1. Bitte klicken Sie den Link um zu Ihrer individuellen Seite zu kommen' || chr(10) ||
                '2. Bitte markieren Sie über die Checkbox alle Vorschriften welche Sie bestätigen oder ablehnen wollen' || chr(10) ||
                '3. Bitte klicken Sie auf "Approve", wenn Sie weiterhin als REV für die genannten Vorschriften verantwortlich sind' || chr(10) ||
                '4. Falls Sie nicht mehr für die Vorschriften als REV verantwortlich sind, klicken Sie bitte auf "Reject" und falls Sie den neuen Regulierungsverantwortlichen kennen, dann teilen Sie uns diesen im System bitte mit' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Link: ' || fCreateRevControlUrl(x.verantwortlicherid, x.wert_hash) || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Vielen Dank für Ihre Unterstützung.';

            -- English Text
            -- lBody_EN := 'Dear ' || x.vorname || ' ' || x.nachname || ',' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
            --     'In process XYZ, it is stipulated that the accuracy of the data must be confirmed quarterly by the regulatory officer.' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
            --     'Please confirm that you are listed as a Regulierungsverantwortlicher (REV) for one or more vehicle technical regulations in the ET-B Regulation Index system.' || chr(10) ||
            --     'Click on the link to be redirected to a form where you can see which regulations you are listed as REV for.' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
            --     'Help for the system can be found directly in the form via the ? icons!' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
            --     '1. Please click the link to go to your individual page' || chr(10) ||
            --     '2. Please check the boxes for all regulations you want to confirm or reject' || chr(10) ||
            --     '3. Please click "Approve" if you continue to be responsible as REV for the listed regulations' || chr(10) ||
            --     '4. If you are no longer responsible as REV for the regulations, please click "" and if you know the new regulatory officer, please inform us in the system' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
            --     'Link: ' || fCreateRevControlUrl(x.verantwortlicherid, x.wert_hash) || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
            --     'Thank you for your support.';

            -- Combine both texts with separator
            lBody := lBody_DE || chr(10) || chr(10);
            -- || '---------------' || chr(10) || chr(10) || lBody_EN;

            -- Create the mail link with escaped characters
            lMailLink := 'mailto:' || x.email || 
                        '?subject=' || fEncode(cSubject) || 
                        '&body=' || fEncode(lBody);
        end loop;

        return lMailLink;
    end fCreateMailLink;



    -- Sending emails Directly without asking

    -- Function to prepare email content
    function fCreateMailContent(aRevKontrollID number) return varchar2 is
        lBody_DE varchar2(4000 char);   
        lBody_EN varchar2(4000 char);   
        lBody varchar2(4000 char);
    begin
        for x in (
            select k.verantwortlicherid, k.wert_hash, v.email, v.vorname, v.nachname
            from t_rev_kontrolle k
            join t_verantwortlicher v on (k.verantwortlicherid = v.verantwortlicherid)
            where k.rev_kontrolle_id = aRevKontrollID
        ) loop
            -- German Text
            lBody_DE := 'Sehr geehrte/r ' || x.vorname || ' ' || x.nachname || ',' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Im Prozess '||'<span style="color:red;">XYZ</span>'||' ist festgelegt, dass quartalsweise die Richtigkeit der Daten vom Regulierungsverantwortlichen bestätigt werden muss.' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Bitte bestätigen Sie, dass Sie im System ET-B Regulation Index für eine oder mehrere fahrzeugtechnische Vorschriften als Regulierungsverantwortlicher (REV) genannt sind.' || chr(10) || 
                'Klicken Sie bitte auf den Link, um zu einer Maske weitergeleitet zu werden, in der Sie sehen können, für welche Vorschriften Sie als REV eingetragen sind.' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Hilfestellungen zum System finden Sie direkt in der Maske über die ? Icons!' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                '1. Bitte klicken Sie den Link um zu Ihrer individuellen Seite zu kommen' || chr(10) ||
                '2. Bitte markieren Sie über die Checkbox alle Vorschriften welche Sie bestätigen oder ablehnen wollen' || chr(10) ||
                '3. Bitte klicken Sie auf '||'<span style="text-decoration:underline;">"<strong>Approve</strong>"</span>'||', wenn Sie weiterhin als REV für die genannten Vorschriften verantwortlich sind' || chr(10) ||
                '4. Falls Sie nicht mehr für die Vorschriften als REV verantwortlich sind, klicken Sie bitte auf '||'<span style="text-decoration:underline;">"<strong>Reject</strong>"</span>'||' und falls Sie den neuen Regulierungsverantwortlichen kennen, dann teilen Sie uns diesen im System bitte mit' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Link: ' || fCreateRevControlUrl(x.verantwortlicherid, x.wert_hash) || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Vielen Dank für Ihre Unterstützung.';

            -- English Text
            lBody_EN := 'Dear ' || x.vorname || ' ' || x.nachname || ',' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'In process '||'<span style="color:red;">XYZ</span>'||' it is stipulated that the accuracy of the data must be confirmed quarterly by the regulatory officer.' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Please confirm that you are listed as a Regulierungsverantwortlicher (REV) for one or more vehicle technical regulations in the ET-B Regulation Index system.' || chr(10) ||
                'Click on the link to be redirected to a form where you can see which regulations you are listed as REV for.' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Help for the system can be found directly in the form via the ? icons!' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                '1. Please click the link to go to your individual page' || chr(10) ||
                '2. Please check the boxes for all regulations you want to confirm or reject' || chr(10) ||
                '3. Please click '||'<span>"<strong>Approve</strong>"</span>'||' if you continue to be responsible as REV for the listed regulations' || chr(10) ||
                '4. If you are no longer responsible as REV for the regulations, please click '||'<span>"<strong>Reject</strong>"</span>'||' and if you know the new regulatory officer, please inform us in the system' || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Link: ' || fCreateRevControlUrl(x.verantwortlicherid, x.wert_hash) || chr(10) || chr(10) ||
                'Thank you for your support.';

            -- Combine both texts
            lBody := lBody_DE || chr(10) || chr(10) || '---------------' || chr(10) || chr(10) || lBody_EN;
        end loop;
        return lBody;
    end fCreateMailContent;

    -- Procedure to send emails


    procedure pSendRevMail(aRevKontrollID in number) is
        lMail number;
        lTo varchar2(250 char);
        lHash t_rev_kontrolle.wert_hash%type;
        lVerantwortlicherID number;
        cFrom constant varchar2(250) := 'keyur-madhusudan.dhotrikar@audi.de';
    begin
    
        for x in (select * from t_rev_mailkonfig) loop
                    
            update t_rev_kontrolle set status = 20, zeitpunkt_versand = sysdate where rev_kontrolle_id = aRevKontrollID;        
        
            if (nvl(x.mail_aktiv,0) = 0) then
                exit;
            end if;            
            
            select k.verantwortlicherid, k.wert_hash, v.email
            into lVerantwortlicherID, lHash, lTo
            from t_rev_kontrolle k
            join t_verantwortlicher v on (k.verantwortlicherid = v.verantwortlicherid)
            where k.rev_kontrolle_id = aRevKontrollID;            
            
            lMail := apex_mail.send(
                p_to => lTo,
                p_from => cFrom,
                p_body => x.mailtext,
                p_body_html => replace(x.mailtext, '#LINK#', fCreateRevControlUrl(lVerantwortlicherID, lHash)),
                p_subj => x.betreff
            );
            
            apex_mail.add_attachment(
                p_mail_id => lMail,
                p_attachment => x.attach_bild,
                p_filename => 'bild_rev.jpg',
                p_mime_type => 'image/jpeg',
                p_content_id => 'inline-image'
            );
            
            commit;
        
        end loop;
 
    end pSendRevMail;








    procedure pConfirmChanges(aRevKontrolleVorschriftID in number) is
        lNeuerVerantwortlicherID number;
        lBisherigerVerantwortlicherID number;
        lGid varchar2(16 char);
        lVorschriftID number;
        lStatus number;
    begin

        select neuer_verantwortlicherid, b.gid, vorschriftid, rkv.status, rk.verantwortlicherid into lNeuerVerantwortlicherID, lGid, lVorschriftID, lStatus, lBisherigerVerantwortlicherID
        from t_rev_kontrolle_vorschrift rkv
        join t_rev_kontrolle rk on (rk.rev_kontrolle_id = rkv.rev_kontrolle_id)
        left outer join t_benutzer b on (b.benutzerid = rkv.neuer_verantwortlicherid)        
        where rev_kontrolle_vorschrift_id = aRevKontrolleVorschriftID;

        -- Verantwortlicher wechselt
        if (lNeuerVerantwortlicherID is not null) then

            merge into t_verantwortlicher v
            using (
                select nachname, vorname, abteilung, email, gid
                from t_benutzer
                where benutzerid = lNeuerVerantwortlicherID
            ) u
            on (v.gid = u.gid)
            when not matched then insert (nachname, vorname, abteilung, email, gid)
            values (u.nachname, u.vorname, u.abteilung, u.email, u.gid);

            select verantwortlicherid into lNeuerVerantwortlicherID
            from t_verantwortlicher
            where gid = lGid;

            update t_vorschrift_ref_verantwortlicher
            set verantwortlicherid = lNeuerVerantwortlicherID
            where vorschriftid = lVorschriftID and verantwortlicherid = lBisherigerVerantwortlicherID;

        end if;

        -- Ablehnung bestätigen
        if (lStatus = 20 and lNeuerVerantwortlicherID is null) then
            delete from t_vorschrift_ref_verantwortlicher
            where vorschriftid = lVorschriftID and verantwortlicherid = lBisherigerVerantwortlicherID;
        end if;

        update t_rev_kontrolle_vorschrift
        set bestaetigung = 1
        where rev_kontrolle_vorschrift_id = aRevKontrolleVorschriftID;


    end pConfirmChanges;












END PCK_REV;

   aListVorschriftId: Durch ':' getrennte Liste von Vorschriften-IDs, 
        bearbeitet werden sollen

        aHomologation, aRxsWin: Neuer Wert der jeweiligen
        Spalte; null = alten Wert behalten
*/

        aBemerkung VARCHAR2, aFreigabeStatusId NUMBER, aEinsatzdatumModellId NUMBER,

        aRxsWin NUMBER) return BOOLEAN;

        null = alten Wert behalten
*/

return boolean;

   aListVorschriftId: Durch ':' getrennte Liste von Vorschriften-IDs, 
        bearbeitet werden sollen

        die gesetzt werden sollen;
        null = alten Wert behalten
*/

return boolean;

/* Ändert bestimmte Links von Vorschriften, *wenn diese noch nicht gesetzt sind*
   aListVorschriftId: Durch ':' getrennte Liste von Vorschriften-IDs, 
        bearbeitet werden sollen
    aLinkGetex, aLinkDms, aWebsiteId, aLinkWebsite: Neuer Wert der jeweiligen
        Spalte; null = alten Wert behalten
*/

        aLinkDms VARCHAR2, aWebsiteId NUMBER, aLinkWebsite VARCHAR2) return BOOLEAN;

    auf ein Zielland für die ausgewählten Vorschriften.

   aListVorschriftId: Durch ':' getrennte Liste von Vorschriften-IDs,

        aSourceLandId NUMBER, aListTargetLandId VARCHAR2) return BOOLEAN;

/* Kopiert de Zuordnungen zu den Laendern von einem Quell-Themengebiet

   aListVorschriftId: Durch ':' getrennte Liste von Vorschriften-IDs,

    aTargetThemaId: Durch ':' getrennte Liste von Ziel-Thema-IDs
*/

        aSourceThemaId NUMBER, aListTargetThemaId VARCHAR2) return BOOLEAN;

function fGetLinks(aVorschriftID in number) return apex_t_number;

/* Ändert bestimmte Eigenschaften von Vorschriften
    aListVorschriftId: Durch ':' getrennte Liste von Vorschriften-IDs, 
        bearbeitet werden sollen
    aAttribut: Numerische Repräsentation der Tabellenspalte
        Vorschriftennummer=10, Titel (Überschrift)=20, Bemerkung zur Vorschrift=30,
        Link zu DMS=40, Link zu GETEX=50, Link zu Web Site=60
    aPlainRegexReplae: Suchen und Erserten via Wortersetzung (0 = plain) oder 
        Regulärem Ausdruck (1)
    aSearchText: Text der gesucht und ersetzt werden soll
    aReplaceText: Text der den alten Text ersetzen soll
*/
function fSearchAndReplaceVorschriftenAttribut(aListVorschriftId VARCHAR2, aAttribut NUMBER,

  die Länder aus der liste  alaenderids  hinzu
*/

create or replace PACKAGE BODY "PCK_RI" AS
 
  g_jira_base_url CONSTANT VARCHAR2(60 CHAR) := 'https://cicd.cloud.audi/jira/browse/';
 
 
    /* Setzt alle vernetzten Informationen für eine Vorschrift zurück */
    procedure pResetVI(aVorschriftID in number) is
    begin
        pResetAK(aVorschriftID);
        pResetAA(aVorschriftID);
        pResetFunktionen(aVorschriftID);        
    end pResetVI;
 
    /* Setzt die Arbeitskreise für eine Vorschrift zurück */
    procedure pResetAK(aVorschriftID in number) is
    begin
 
        update t_vorschrift_ref_et_b_ak
        set geloescht = 1, letzte_aenderung_datum = sysdate, letzte_aenderung_benutzerid = fGetUserId
        where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID 
        and et_b_akid not in (
            select distinct et_b_akid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_thema vrt
            join t_thema_ref_et_b_ak ref on (vrt.themaid = ref.themaid)
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID and geloescht = 0
        );            
 
        update t_vorschrift_ref_et_b_ak
        set geloescht = 0, letzte_aenderung_datum = sysdate, letzte_aenderung_benutzerid = fGetUserId
        where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID
        and et_b_akid in (
            select distinct et_b_akid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_thema vrt
            join t_thema_ref_et_b_ak ref on (vrt.themaid = ref.themaid)
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID and geloescht = 0
        );
 
        insert into t_vorschrift_ref_et_b_ak (
            vorschriftid, et_b_akid, letzte_aenderung_benutzerid, letzte_aenderung_datum
        )
        with cte1 as (
            select distinct et_b_akid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_thema vrt
            join t_thema_ref_et_b_ak ref on (vrt.themaid = ref.themaid)
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID and geloescht = 0
        )
        select aVorschriftID, et_b_akid, fGetUserId, sysdate
        from cte1
        where et_b_akid not in (
            select et_b_akid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_et_b_ak
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID
        );
 
    end pResetAK;
 
    /* Setzt die Antriebsarten für eine Vorschrift zurück */
    procedure pResetAA(aVorschriftID in number) is
     l_co number :=0;
     l_aa_co number :=0;
     l_insert_co number :=0;
    begin
        -- prüfe Änderungen in Getex-relevantem Attribut AntriebsArt
        select count(*) into l_co from t_vorschrift_ref_antriebsart
        where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID;
 
        select count(distinct antriebsartid) into l_aa_co
            from t_vorschrift_ref_thema vrt
            join t_thema_ref_antriebsart ref on (vrt.themaid = ref.themaid)
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID and vrt.geloescht = 0;
        --
        update t_vorschrift_ref_antriebsart
        set geloescht = 0, letzte_aenderung_datum = sysdate, letzte_aenderung_benutzerid = fGetUserId
        where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID
        and antriebsartid in (
            select distinct antriebsartid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_thema vrt
            join t_thema_ref_antriebsart ref on (vrt.themaid = ref.themaid)
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID and geloescht = 0
        );
 
        with cte1 as (
            select distinct antriebsartid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_thema vrt
            join t_thema_ref_antriebsart ref on (vrt.themaid = ref.themaid)
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID and geloescht = 0
        )
        select  count(antriebsartid) into l_insert_co
        from cte1
        where antriebsartid not in (
            select antriebsartid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_antriebsart
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID
        );
 
        insert into t_vorschrift_ref_antriebsart (
            vorschriftid, antriebsartid, letzte_aenderung_benutzerid, letzte_aenderung_datum
        )
        with cte1 as (
            select distinct antriebsartid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_thema vrt
            join t_thema_ref_antriebsart ref on (vrt.themaid = ref.themaid)
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID and geloescht = 0
        )
        select aVorschriftID, antriebsartid, fGetUserId, sysdate
        from cte1
        where antriebsartid not in (
            select antriebsartid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_antriebsart
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID
        );
 
         if( (l_co >0 and l_aa_co >0) or l_insert_co >0 ) then
          update t_vorschrift set letzte_aenderung_getex_attr =sysdate  where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID;
        end if;
    end pResetAA;
 
    /* Setzt die FUKA-Funktionen für eine Vorschrift zurück */
    procedure pResetFunktionen(aVorschriftID in number) is
    begin
        /* zugeordnete Funktionen, die als gelöscht markiert waren, wiederherstellen, wenn sie zum
           Standardprogramm der zugeordneten Themen gehören */
        update t_vorschrift_ref_funktion
        set geloescht = 0, letzte_aenderung_datum = sysdate, letzte_aenderung_benutzerid = fGetUserId
        where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID
        and geloescht = 1
        and funktionid in (
            select distinct funktionid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_thema vrt
            join t_thema_ref_funktion ref on (vrt.themaid = ref.themaid)
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID and geloescht = 0
        );
 
        /* zugeordnete Funktionen als gelöscht markieren, wenn sie nicht zum Standardprogramm der
           zugeordneten Themen gehören 
           Änderung TsTh 18.01.: Zusätzlich zugeordnete Funktionen sollen nicht mehr als gelöscht markiert werden 
 
            update t_vorschrift_ref_funktion
            set geloescht = 1, letzte_aenderung_datum = sysdate, letzte_aenderung_benutzerid = fGetUserId
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID
            and geloescht = 0
            and funktionid not in (
                select distinct funktionid
                from t_vorschrift_ref_thema_ref_land vrt
                join t_thema_ref_funktion ref on (vrt.themaid = ref.themaid)
                where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID and geloescht = 0
            );   
 
        */
 
        /* Funktionen aus dem Standardprogramm der Themen zuordnen, wenn noch nicht da */
        insert into t_vorschrift_ref_funktion (
            vorschriftid, funktionid, letzte_aenderung_benutzerid, letzte_aenderung_datum
        )
        with cte1 as (
            select distinct funktionid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_thema vrt
            join t_thema_ref_funktion ref on (vrt.themaid = ref.themaid)
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID and geloescht = 0
        )
        select aVorschriftID, funktionid, fGetUserId, sysdate
        from cte1
        where funktionid not in (
            select funktionid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_funktion
            where vorschriftid = aVorschriftID
        );
    end pResetFunktionen;
 
  function fSanitizeForTree(aText in varchar2) return varchar2 is
  begin    
      return trim(replace(replace(replace(aText,'"'),chr(10)),chr(13)));
  end fSanitizeForTree;
 
  FUNCTION fGetUserId return NUMBER AS
  BEGIN
    RETURN V('G_BENUTZERID');
  END fGetUserId;
 
    function fGetLinks(aVorschriftID in number) return apex_t_number is
        lReturnList apex_t_number;   
 
    begin
        with cte1 as (
            select vrv.nachfolger_vorschriftid vorschriftid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_vorschrift vrv
            where vrv.vorgaenger_vorschriftid = aVorschriftID
            union
            select vrv.vorgaenger_vorschriftid
            from t_vorschrift_ref_vorschrift vrv
            where vrv.nachfolger_vorschriftid = aVorschriftID
        )
        select vorschriftid
        bulk collect into lReturnList
        from cte1;
        return lReturnList;
 
 
    end fGetLinks;
 
    FUNCTION fIsAuthorized01(userId NUMBER default fGetUserId, pageId NUMBER, accessMode NUMBER) return number
    is begin
        if (fIsAuthorized(userid, pageid, accessmode)) then
            return 1;
        else
            return 0;
        end if;
 
    end fIsAuthorized01;
 
    /* Liefert 1 zurück, wenn es sich um einen anonymen oder deaktivierten User handelt
       --> nur freigegebene Vorschriften sichtbar */
    function fIsLimitedUser(userId number default fGetUserId) return number is
        lUserStatus number;
        lGruppenAusserSuche number;
    begin
 
        if (userID is null) then
            return 1;
        else
            select status into lUserStatus
            from t_benutzer
            where benutzerid = userId;
 
            select count(*) into lGruppenAusserSuche
            from t_benutzer_ref_rolle
            where benutzerid = userid and rolleid  not in ( 1004, 1005);
 
            if (lUserStatus = 20 or lGruppenAusserSuche = 0) then
                return 1;
            end if;
        end if;
 
        return 0;
 
 
 
    end fIsLimitedUser;

        260, 265, 280, 281, 282, 286,
        343,
        410, 415, 416, 420, 421, 423, 425,
        2000, 2005
      )
 
      union all
 
      select 'Inaktive Funktionen' as role_name, 100 as userright, column_value as page_id from sys.odcinumberlist(
         20, 21, 25, 31, 460, 461, 462, 463, 481, 486,
         540, 541, 542, 543, 544, 545
      )
      union all
      select 'Inaktive Funktionen' as role_name, 200 as userright, column_value as page_id from sys.odcinumberlist(
            25, 31, 460, 461, 462, 463, 481, 486,
            540, 541, 542, 543, 544, 545
      )      
    )
    Select count(*) into lResult from access_rules ar
    join T_ROLLE r on r.ROLLE = ar.role_name 
    join T_BENUTZER_REF_ROLLE brr on brr.rolleid = r.rolleid
    join T_BENUTZER b on b.benutzerid = brr.benutzerid
    where b.benutzerid = userId and ar.userright=accessMode and ar.page_id = pageId and b.status = 10;
 
    RETURN lResult > 0;
 
  END fIsAuthorized;
 
 */
 
  -- Ermittlung ob der Benutzer auf die Seite lesend oder schreibend zugreifen darf
  -- accessMode: 100 lesend, 200 schreibend, 300 Admin only
  FUNCTION fIsAuthorized(userId NUMBER default fGetUserId, pageId NUMBER, accessMode NUMBER) return BOOLEAN IS
    lResult NUMBER;
    lIsAdmin NUMBER;
  BEGIN
    lResult := 0;
    lIsAdmin := 0;
    -- Shortcut für Mynet User ohne eigenen Account, deaktivierte Accounts
    -- bzw. Seiten, die jeder immer aufrufen darf
    IF accessMode = 100  
            and pageId in (0, 1,2,  5, 9,11,20, 21, 23, 25, 31, 28, 30, 65, 70, 
            130, 136, 200, 202, 210, 251, 280, 281, 282, 286,
            300, 320, 322, 323, 325, 326, 327, 340, 341, 366, 367, 380, 390, 
            400,  410,   -- 420, 425, 
            440, 450, 452, 455, 457, 456, 457, 459,
            520,
            600,601,603,605,617, 630,660,
            2010, 2400
            -- REGINDEXE-1376
             ) THEN
        return TRUE;
    END IF;
 
    -- Shortcut fuer Admin User: Immer alle Rechte
    /*select count(*) INTO lIsAdmin from T_BENUTZER b
    join T_BENUTZER_REF_ROLLE brr on brr.benutzerid = b.benutzerid
    where brr.benutzerid = userId 
      AND brr.rolleid = g_rolleid_admin 
      AND b.status = 10; -- 10: Benutzer aktiv
 
    IF lIsAdmin > 0 THEN
        return TRUE;
    END IF;*/
 
    -- Erstellt eine Tabelle access_rules mit Rollennamen (role_name), Benutzerrecht (userrigth)
    -- und den berechteten Seiten (page_id) 
    -- und selektiert daraus die Zeile(n) bei der Rolle, Seite und Benutzerrecht uebereinstimmen.
    with access_rules as (
      select 'Fachadmin' as role_name, 100 as userright, column_value as page_id from sys.odcinumberlist(
        0, 1, 10, 15, 16, 20, 21,23, 25, 31, 26, 27, 28, 29, 30, 33, 35, 36, 38, 44, 45, 46, 60, 65, 70, 75, 80, 85, 90, 95, 96,

        400, 410, 415, 416, 420, 421, 423, 425, 430, 440, 450, 452, 453, 455, 456, 457, 458, 459, 470, 472, 474, 480, 481, 485, 486,
        510, 515, 520, 521, 530, 541, 542, 543, 544, 545, 570, 571, 572, 573, 574, 575, 578,581,582, 590, 595,
         603, 610, 615, 617, 630, 640,645, 650, 655,
        700, 701,702,703, 705, 706, 710, 715, 720, 725, 730, 735,
        800, 810,820,
        900, 905, 910, 915, 920, 925, 926, 927, 928, 929, 930, 935, 940, 945, 950, 955, 960, 970,
        1000, 1010,1015, 1100,
